<pr_description>
[Bug]: Installing from a ckan file has issues with suggests or recommends stanza having conflicts
### Is there an existing issue for this?

- [x] I have checked the existing issues for an existing issue. I even actually looked at the ones that are pinned to the top!

### Operating System

Win-11

### CKAN Version

1.36.3.26017

### Games

KSP 1

### Game Version

1.12.5

### Did you make any manual changes to your game folder (i.e., not via CKAN)?

_No response_

### Describe the bug

Having a "recommends" or a "suggests" stanza in the ckan will cause any mods which are listed as a conflict in an earlier line to hide the later ones.

### Steps to reproduce

Create a .ckan export
Add the following: to the end, following the "depends" stanza

```json
  "recommends": [
            { "name": "KcalbelohSystem" },
            { "name": "PromisedWorldsCore" },
            { "name": "JNSQ" },
            { "name": "GPP" },
            { "name": "OuterPlanetsMod" }
      ]
```

Try to install from the ckan.
The following mods will be shown in the Recommendations line:
    JNSQ
    Kcalbeloh System
    Promised Worlds Core

Moving JNSQ after the GPP line will show the following:
    Galileio's Planet Pack
    Kcalbeloh System
    Outer Planets Mod
    Promised Worlds - Core

I would have expected all the mods to be listed, and if two selected which have a conflict, to show them in red

### Relevant log output

_No response_

2026-05-29 15:11:25,109 - DEBUG - swea-tools-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - Retrieved state from environment: {}
2026-05-29 15:11:25,111 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

     1	using System;
     2	using System.Collections.Generic;
     3	using System.Linq;
     4	
     5	using log4net;
     6	
     7	using CKAN.Configuration;
     8	using CKAN.Games;
     9	using CKAN.Versioning;
    10	using CKAN.Extensions;
    11	
    12	namespace CKAN
    13	{
    14	    using ModPair = KeyValuePair<CkanModule, CkanModule?>;
    15	
    16	    /// <summary>
    17	    /// Resolves relationships between mods. Primarily used to satisfy missing dependencies and to check for conflicts on proposed installs.
    18	    /// </summary>
    19	    public class RelationshipResolver
    20	    {
    21	        /// <summary>
    22	        /// Creates a new resolver that will find a way to install all the modules specified.
    23	        /// </summary>
    24	        /// <param name="modulesToInstall">Modules to install</param>
    25	        /// <param name="modulesToRemove">Modules to remove</param>
    26	        /// <param name="options">Options for the RelationshipResolver</param>
    27	        /// <param name="registry">CKAN registry object for current game instance</param>
    28	        /// <param name="game">The game to mention in error messages</param>
    29	        /// <param name="versionCrit">The current game version criteria to consider</param>
    30	        public RelationshipResolver(IEnumerable<CkanModule>     modulesToInstall,
    31	                                    IEnumerable<CkanModule>?    modulesToRemove,
    32	                                    RelationshipResolverOptions options,
    33	                                    IRegistryQuerier            registry,
    34	                                    IGame                       game,
    35	                                    GameVersionCriteria         versionCrit)
    36	        {
    37	            this.options     = options;
    38	            this.registry    = registry;
    39	            this.game        = game;
    40	            this.versionCrit = versionCrit;
    41	
    42	            installed_modules = registry.InstalledModules
    43	                                        .Select(i_module => i_module.Module)
    44	                                        .Except(modulesToRemove ?? Enumerable.Empty<CkanModule>())
    45	                                        .ToHashSet();
    46	            var installed_relationship = new SelectionReason.Installed();
    47	            foreach (var module in installed_modules)
    48	            {
    49	                AddReason(module, installed_relationship);
    50	            }
    51	
    52	            var toInst = modulesToInstall.ToArray();
    53	            // DLLs that we are upgrading to full modules should be excluded
    54	            dlls = registry.InstalledDlls
    55	                           .Except(modulesToInstall.Select(m => m.identifier))
    56	                           .ToHashSet();
    57	            resolved = new ResolvedRelationshipsTree(toInst, registry, dlls,
    58	                                                     installed_modules,
    59	                                                     options.stability_tolerance ?? new StabilityToleranceConfig(""),
    60	                                                     versionCrit,
    61	                                                     options.OptionalHandling());
    62	            if (!options.proceed_with_inconsistencies
    63	                && resolved.Unsatisfied().ToArray() is { Length: > 0 } unsatisfied)
    64	            {
    65	                log.DebugFormat("Dependencies failed!{0}{0}{1}{0}{0}{2}",
    66	                                Environment.NewLine,
    67	                                Environment.StackTrace,
    68	                                resolved);
    69	                throw new DependenciesNotSatisfiedKraken(unsatisfied, registry, game, resolved);
    70	            }
    71	
    72	            AddModulesToInstall(toInst);
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        /// <summary>
    76	        /// Add modules to consideration of the relationship resolver.
    77	        /// </summary>
    78	        /// <param name="modules">Modules to attempt to install</param>
    79	        private void AddModulesToInstall(CkanModule[] modules)
    80	        {
    81	            log.DebugFormat("Processing relationships for {0} modules", modules.Length);
    82	
    83	            // Start by figuring out what versions we're installing, and then
    84	            // adding them to the list. This *must* be pre-populated with all
    85	            // user-specified modules, as they may be supplying things that provide
    86	            // virtual packages.
    87	
    88	            // This part can't be parallel, to preserve order of processing
    89	            foreach (CkanModule module in modules)
    90	            {
    91	                log.DebugFormat("Preparing to resolve relationships for {0} {1}", module.identifier, module.version);
    92	
    93	                // Need to check against installed mods and those to install.
    94	                var conflictingModules = modlist.Values
    95	                                                .Concat(installed_modules)
    96	                                                .Where(listed_mod => listed_mod.ConflictsWith(module));
    97	                foreach (CkanModule listed_mod in conflictingModules)
    98	                {
    99	                    if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
   100	                    {
   101	                        conflicts.Add(new ModPair(listed_mod, module));
   102	                        conflicts.Add(new ModPair(module, listed_mod));
   103	                    }
   104	                    else
   105	                    {
   106	                        throw new InconsistentKraken(string.Format(
   107	                            Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictsWith,
   108	                            module, listed_mod));
   109	                    }
   110	                }
   111	
   112	                user_requested_mods.Add(module);
   113	                Add(module, new SelectionReason.UserRequested());
   114	            }
   115	
   116	            // Now that we've already pre-populated the modlist, we can resolve
   117	            // the rest of our dependencies.
   118	
   119	            foreach (var module in user_requested_mods)
   120	            {
   121	                log.DebugFormat("Resolving relationships for {0}", module.identifier);
   122	                Resolve(module, options);
   123	            }
   124	
   125	            try
   126	            {
   127	                // Check that our solution is actually sane
   128	                SanityChecker.EnforceConsistency(modlist.Values.Concat(installed_modules),
   129	                                                 dlls,
   130	                                                 registry.InstalledDlc);
   131	            }
   132	            catch (BadRelationshipsKraken k) when (options.without_enforce_consistency)
   133	            {
   134	                conflicts.AddRange(k.Conflicts.Select(tuple => new ModPair(tuple.Item1, tuple.Item3))
   135	                                              .Where(pair => !conflicts.Contains(pair))
   136	                                              .ToArray());
   137	            }
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        /// <summary>
   141	        /// Resolves all relationships for a module.
   142	        /// May recurse to ResolveStanza, which may add additional modules to be installed.
   143	        /// </summary>
   144	        private void Resolve(CkanModule                           module,
   145	                             RelationshipResolverOptions          options,
   146	                             IEnumerable<RelationshipDescriptor>? old_stanza = null)
   147	        {
   148	            if (alreadyResolved.Contains(module))
   149	            {
   150	                return;
   151	            }
   152	            // Mark this module as resolved so we don't recurse here again
   153	            alreadyResolved.Add(module);
   154	
   155	            old_stanza = old_stanza?.Memoize();
   156	
   157	            log.DebugFormat("Resolving dependencies for {0}", module.identifier);
   158	            ResolveStanza(module.depends, new SelectionReason.Depends(module), options, false, old_stanza);
   159	
   160	            // TODO: RR currently conducts a depth-first resolution of requirements. While we do the
   161	            // right thing in processing all dependencies first, then recommends, and then suggests,
   162	            // we could find that a recommendation many layers deep prevents a recommendation in the
   163	            // original mod's recommends list.
   164	            //
   165	            // If we resolved in things breadth-first order, we're less likely to encounter surprises
   166	            // where a nth-deep recommend blocks a top-level recommend.
   167	
   168	            if (options.with_recommends)
   169	            {
   170	                log.DebugFormat("Resolving recommends for {0}", module.identifier);
   171	                ResolveStanza(module.recommends, new SelectionReason.Recommended(module, 0),
   172	                              options.get_recommenders ? options.WithoutRecommendations()
   173	                                                       : options.WithoutSuggestions(),
   174	                              true, old_stanza);
   175	            }
   176	
   177	            if (options.with_suggests || options.with_all_suggests)
   178	            {
   179	                log.DebugFormat("Resolving suggests for {0}", module.identifier);
   180	                ResolveStanza(module.suggests, new SelectionReason.Suggested(module),
   181	                              options.get_recommenders ? options.WithoutRecommendations()
   182	                                                       : options.WithoutSuggestions(),
   183	                              true, old_stanza);
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	
   187	        /// <summary>
   188	        /// Resolve a relationship stanza (a list of relationships).
   189	        /// This will add modules to be installed, if required.
   190	        /// May recurse back to Resolve for those new modules.
   191	        ///
   192	        /// If `soft_resolve` is true, we warn rather than throw exceptions on mods we cannot find.
   193	        /// If `soft_resolve` is false (default), we throw a ModuleNotFoundKraken if we can't find a dependency.
   194	        ///
   195	        /// Throws a TooManyModsProvideKraken if we have too many choices and
   196	        /// options.without_toomanyprovides_kraken is not set.
   197	        ///
   198	        /// See RelationshipResolverOptions for further adjustments that can be made.
   199	        /// </summary>
   200	        private void ResolveStanza(List<RelationshipDescriptor>?        stanza,
   201	                                   SelectionReason                      reason,
   202	                                   RelationshipResolverOptions          options,
   203	                                   bool                                 soft_resolve,
   204	                                   IEnumerable<RelationshipDescriptor>? old_stanza)
   205	        {
   206	            if (stanza == null)
   207	            {
   208	                return;
   209	            }
   210	
   211	            var orig_options = options;
   212	            foreach (RelationshipDescriptor descriptor in stanza)
   213	            {
   214	                log.DebugFormat("Considering {0}", descriptor.ToString());
   215	
   216	                if (options.get_recommenders && descriptor.suppress_recommendations)
   217	                {
   218	                    log.DebugFormat("Skipping {0} because get_recommenders option is set",
   219	                                    descriptor.ToString());
   220	                    suppressedRecommenders.Add(descriptor);
   221	                    continue;
   222	                }
   223	                options = orig_options.OptionsFor(descriptor);
   224	
   225	                // If we already have this dependency covered,
   226	                // resolve its relationships if we haven't already
   227	                if (descriptor.MatchesAny(modlist.Values, null, null,
   228	                                          out CkanModule? installingCandidate)
   229	                    && installingCandidate != null)
   230	                {
   231	                    log.DebugFormat("Match already in changeset: {0}, adding reason {1}",
   232	                                    installingCandidate, reason);
   233	                    AddReason(installingCandidate, reason);
   234	                    // Resolve the relationships of the matching module here
   235	                    // because that's when it would happen if non-virtual
   236	                    Resolve(installingCandidate, options, stanza);
   237	                    continue;
   238	                }
   239	                if (descriptor.ContainsAny(modlist.Keys))
   240	                {
   241	                    // Two installing mods depend on different versions of this dependency
   242	                    var module = modlist.Values.FirstOrDefault(m => descriptor.ContainsAny(new string[] { m.identifier }));
   243	                    log.DebugFormat("Changeset contains {0}, which doesn't match {1}",
   244	                                    module, descriptor.ToString());
   245	                    if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
   246	                    {
   247	                        if (module != null && reason is SelectionReason.RelationshipReason rel)
   248	                        {
   249	                            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(module, rel.Parent));
   250	                            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(rel.Parent, module));
   251	                        }
   252	                        continue;
   253	                    }
   254	                    else
   255	                    {
   256	                        throw new InconsistentKraken(string.Format(
   257	                            Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverRequiredButResolver,
   258	                            descriptor));
   259	                    }
   260	                }
   261	
   262	                // If it's already installed, skip.
   263	                if (descriptor.MatchesAny(installed_modules,
   264	                                          dlls,
   265	                                          registry.InstalledDlc,
   266	                                          out CkanModule? installedCandidate))
   267	                {
   268	                    if (installedCandidate != null)
   269	                    {
   270	                        log.DebugFormat("Match already installed: {0}, adding reason {1}",
   271	                                        installedCandidate, reason);
   272	                        AddReason(installedCandidate, reason);
   273	                    }
   274	                    else
   275	                    {
   276	                        log.DebugFormat("Matches installed DLL or DLC");
   277	                    }
   278	                    continue;
   279	                }
   280	
   281	                IReadOnlyList<CkanModule>? candidates = null;
   282	                try
   283	                {
   284	                    candidates = resolved.Candidates(descriptor, modlist.Values,
   285	                                                     registry, game);
   286	                    log.DebugFormat("Got {0} candidates for {1}",
   287	                                    candidates.Count, descriptor);
   288	                }
   289	                catch
   290	                when (soft_resolve || options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
   291	                {
   292	                    log.InfoFormat("{0} is recommended/suggested but it is not listed in the index, or not available for your game version.",
   293	                                   descriptor);
   294	                    continue;
   295	                }
   296	
   297	                if (candidates.Count > 1)
   298	                {
   299	                    // Oh no, too many to pick from!
   300	                    if (options.without_toomanyprovides_kraken)
   301	                    {
   302	                        if (options.get_recommenders && reason is not SelectionReason.Depends)
   303	                        {
   304	                            for (int i = 0; i < candidates.Count; ++i)
   305	                            {
   306	                                Add(candidates[i], reason is SelectionReason.Recommended rec
   307	                                                       ? rec.WithIndex(i)
   308	                                                       : reason);
   309	                            }
   310	                        }
   311	                        continue;
   312	                    }
   313	
   314	                    // If we've got a parent stanza that has a relationship on a mod that provides what
   315	                    // we need, then select that.
   316	                    if (old_stanza != null)
   317	                    {
   318	                        var provide = candidates.Where(c => old_stanza.Any(rel => rel.WithinBounds(c)))
   319	                                                .ToArray();
   320	                        if (provide.Length != 1 && reason is SelectionReason.RelationshipReason rel)
   321	                        {
   322	                            // We still have either nothing, or too many to pick from
   323	                            // Just throw the TMP now
   324	                            throw new TooManyModsProvideKraken(rel.Parent, descriptor.ToString() ?? "",
   325	                                                               candidates, descriptor.choice_help_text);
   326	                        }
   327	                        candidates = new List<CkanModule> { provide.First() };
   328	                    }
   329	                    else if (reason is SelectionReason.RelationshipReason rel)
   330	                    {
   331	                        throw new TooManyModsProvideKraken(rel.Parent, descriptor.ToString() ?? "",
   332	                                                           candidates, descriptor.choice_help_text);
   333	                    }
   334	                }
   335	
   336	                CkanModule candidate = candidates.Single();
   337	
   338	                // Finally, check our candidate against everything which might object
   339	                // to it being installed; that's all the mods which are fixed in our
   340	                // list thus far, as well as everything on the system.
   341	                var fixed_mods = modlist.Values.Concat(installed_modules).ToHashSet();
   342	
   343	                var conflicting_mod = fixed_mods.FirstOrDefault(mod => mod.ConflictsWith(candidate));
   344	                if (conflicting_mod == null)
   345	                {
   346	                    // Okay, looks like we want this one. Adding.
   347	                    Add(candidate,
   348	                        descriptor is ModuleRelationshipDescriptor rel
   349	                        && rel.name != candidate.identifier
   350	                        && reason is SelectionReason.Depends depRsn
   351	                               ? new SelectionReason.VirtualDepends(depRsn.Parent,
   352	                                                                    descriptor.ToString() ?? "")
   353	                               : reason);
   354	                    Resolve(candidate, options, stanza);
   355	                }
   356	                else if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
   357	                {
   358	                    Add(candidate, reason);
   359	                    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(conflicting_mod, candidate));
   360	                    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(candidate, conflicting_mod));
   361	                }
   362	                else if (soft_resolve)
   363	                {
   364	                    log.InfoFormat("{0} would cause conflicts, excluding it from consideration", candidate);
   365	                }
   366	                else
   367	                {
   368	                    throw new InconsistentKraken(string.Format(
   369	                        Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictsWith,
   370	                        conflictingModDescription(conflicting_mod, null),
   371	                        conflictingModDescription(candidate, (reason as SelectionReason.RelationshipReason)?.Parent)));
   372	                }
   373	            }
   374	        }
   375	
   376	        private string conflictingModDescription(CkanModule? mod, CkanModule? parent)
   377	            => mod == null
   378	                ? Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverAnUnmanaged
   379	                : parent == null && ReasonsFor(mod).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.UserRequested
   380	                                                               or SelectionReason.Installed)
   381	                    // No parenthetical needed if it's user requested
   382	                    ? mod.ToString()
   383	                    // Explain why we're looking at this mod
   384	                    : string.Format(Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictingModDescription,
   385	                                    mod.ToString(),
   386	                                    string.Join(", ", UserReasonsFor(parent ?? mod).Select(m => m.ToString())));
   387	
   388	        /// <summary>
   389	        /// Adds the specified module to the list of modules we're installing.
   390	        /// This also adds its provides list to what we have available.
   391	        /// </summary>
   392	        private void Add(CkanModule module, SelectionReason reason)
   393	        {
   394	            log.DebugFormat("Adding {0} {1}", module.identifier, module.version);
   395	
   396	            if (modlist.TryGetValue(module.identifier, out CkanModule? possibleDup))
   397	            {
   398	                if (possibleDup.identifier == module.identifier)
   399	                {
   400	                    if (possibleDup.version == module.version
   401	                        && !possibleDup.MetadataEquals(module))
   402	                    {
   403	                        // If the version is the same and the metadata changed,
   404	                        // queue this up as a reinstall (remove the old version)
   405	                        reasons.Remove(possibleDup);
   406	                        modlist.Remove(possibleDup.identifier);
   407	                    }
   408	                    else
   409	                    {
   410	                        // We should never add the same module twice!
   411	                        log.ErrorFormat("Assertion failed: Already added {0}, can't add {1} ({2})",
   412	                                        possibleDup, module, reason);
   413	                        throw new ArgumentException($"Already added {possibleDup}, can't add {module} ({reason})");
   414	                    }
   415	                }
   416	                else
   417	                {
   418	                    // Duplicates via "provides" are OK though, we'll just replace it
   419	                    modlist.Remove(module.identifier);
   420	                }
   421	            }
   422	            modlist.Add(module.identifier, module);
   423	            AddReason(module, reason);
   424	
   425	            log.DebugFormat("Added {0}", module.identifier);
   426	            // Stop here if it doesn't have any provide aliases.
   427	            if (module.provides == null)
   428	            {
   429	                return;
   430	            }
   431	
   432	            // Handle provides/aliases if it does.
   433	
   434	            // It's okay if there's already a key for one of our aliases
   435	            // in the resolution list. In which case, we don't do anything.
   436	            var aliases = module.provides.Where(alias => !modlist.ContainsKey(alias));
   437	            foreach (string alias in aliases)
   438	            {
   439	                log.DebugFormat("Adding {0} providing {1}", module.identifier, alias);
   440	                modlist.Add(alias, module);
   441	            }
   442	        }
   443	
   444	        /// <summary>
   445	        /// Returns a list of all modules to install to satisfy the changes required.
   446	        /// Each mod is after its dependencies and before its reverse dependencies.
   447	        /// </summary>
   448	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> ModList(bool parallel = true)
   449	            => modlist.Values.Distinct()
   450	                             .AsParallelIf(parallel)
   451	                             // Put user choices at the bottom; .OrderBy(bool) -> false first
   452	                             .OrderBy(m => ReasonsFor(m).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.UserRequested))
   453	                             // Put dependencies before dependers
   454	                             .ThenByDescending(totalDependers)
   455	                             // Resolve ties in name order
   456	                             .ThenBy(m => m.name);
   457	
   458	        public bool ReadyToInstall(CkanModule                      mod,
   459	                                   IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule> installed)
   460	            => !modlist.Values.Distinct()
   461	                              .Where(m => m != mod)
   462	                              .Except(installed)
   463	                              // Ignore circular dependencies
   464	                              .Except(allDependers(mod))
   465	                              .SelectMany(allDependers)
   466	                              .Contains(mod);
   467	
   468	        // The more nodes of the reverse-dependency graph we can paint, the higher up in the list it goes
   469	        private int totalDependers(CkanModule module)
   470	            => allDependers(module).Count();
   471	
   472	        private static IEnumerable<T> BreadthFirstSearch<T>(IEnumerable<T>                      startingGroup,
   473	                                                            Func<T, HashSet<T>, IEnumerable<T>> getNextGroup)
   474	        {
   475	            var found    = startingGroup.ToHashSet();
   476	            var toSearch = new Queue<T>(found);
   477	
   478	            while (toSearch.Count > 0)
   479	            {
   480	                var searching = toSearch.Dequeue();
   481	                yield return searching;
   482	                foreach (var nextNode in getNextGroup(searching, found))
   483	                {
   484	                    found.Add(nextNode);
   485	                    toSearch.Enqueue(nextNode);
   486	                }
   487	            }
   488	        }
   489	
   490	        private IEnumerable<CkanModule> allDependers(CkanModule module)
   491	            => BreadthFirstSearch(Enumerable.Repeat(module, 1),
   492	                                  (searching, found) =>
   493	                                      ReasonsFor(searching).OfType<SelectionReason.RelationshipReason>()
   494	                                                           .Select(r => r.Parent)
   495	                                                           .OfType<CkanModule>()
   496	                                                           .Except(found));
   497	
   498	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Dependencies()
   499	            => BreadthFirstSearch(user_requested_mods.Where(m => !suppressedRecommenders.Any(rel => rel.WithinBounds(m))),
   500	                                  (searching, found) =>
   501	                                      modlist.Values
   502	                                             .Except(found)
   503	                                             .Where(m => ReasonsFor(m).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.Depends dep
   504	                                                                                && dep.Parent == searching)));
   505	
   506	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Recommendations(HashSet<CkanModule> dependencies)
   507	            => modlist.Values.Except(dependencies)
   508	                             .Where(m => ValidRecSugReasons(dependencies,
   509	                                                            ReasonsFor(m).OfType<SelectionReason.Recommended>()
   510	                                                                         .ToArray()))
   511	                             .OrderByDescending(totalDependers);
   512	
   513	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Suggestions(HashSet<CkanModule>             dependencies,
   514	                                                   IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule> recommendations)
   515	            => modlist.Values.Except(dependencies)
   516	                             .Except(recommendations)
   517	                             .Where(m => ValidRecSugReasons(dependencies,
   518	                                                            ReasonsFor(m).OfType<SelectionReason.Suggested>()
   519	                                                                         .ToArray()))
   520	                             .OrderByDescending(totalDependers);
   521	
   522	        private bool ValidRecSugReasons(HashSet<CkanModule>                  dependencies,
   523	                                        SelectionReason.RelationshipReason[] recSugReasons)
   524	            => recSugReasons.Any(r => dependencies.Contains(r.Parent))
   525	               && !suppressedRecommenders.Any(rel => recSugReasons.Any(r => r.Parent != null
   526	                                                                            && rel.WithinBounds(r.Parent)));
   527	
   528	        public ParallelQuery<KeyValuePair<CkanModule, HashSet<string>>> Supporters(
   529	            HashSet<CkanModule>     supported,
   530	            IEnumerable<CkanModule> toExclude)
   531	            => registry.CompatibleModules(options.stability_tolerance ?? new StabilityToleranceConfig(""),
   532	                                          versionCrit)
   533	                       .Except(toExclude)
   534	                       .AsParallel()
   535	                       // Find installable modules with "supports" relationships
   536	                       .Where(mod => !registry.IsInstalled(mod.identifier)
   537	                                     && mod.supports != null)
   538	                       // Find each module that "supports" something we're installing
   539	                       .Select(mod => new KeyValuePair<CkanModule, HashSet<string>>(
   540	                                          mod,
   541	                                          (mod.supports ?? Enumerable.Empty<RelationshipDescriptor>())
   542	                                             .Where(rel => rel.MatchesAny(supported, null, null))
   543	                                             .Select(rel => (rel as ModuleRelationshipDescriptor)?.name)
   544	                                             .OfType<string>()
   545	                                             .Where(name => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(name))
   546	                                             .ToHashSet()))
   547	                       .Where(kvp => kvp.Value.Count > 0);
   548	
   549	        /// <summary>
   550	        /// Returns a dictionary consisting of KeyValuePairs containing conflicting mods.
   551	        /// The keys are the mods that the user chose that led to the conflict being in the list!
   552	        /// Use this for coloring/labelling rows, use ConflictDescriptions for reporting the conflicts to the user.
   553	        /// </summary>
   554	        public Dictionary<CkanModule, string> ConflictList
   555	            => conflicts
   556	                .SelectMany(kvp => UserReasonsFor(kvp.Key).Select(k => new KeyValuePair<CkanModule, ModPair>(k, kvp)))
   557	                .GroupBy(kvp => kvp.Key)
   558	                .ToDictionary(group => group.Key,
   559	                              group => string.Join(", ", group.Select(kvp => kvp.Value)
   560	                                                              .Distinct()
   561	                                                              .Select(origKvp => string.Format(
   562	                        Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictsWith,
   563	                        conflictingModDescription(origKvp.Key, null),
   564	                        conflictingModDescription(origKvp.Value, null)))));
   565	
   566	        /// <summary>
   567	        /// Return descriptions of all the current conflicts.
   568	        /// Avoids duplicates and explains why dependencies are in the list.
   569	        /// Use for reporting the conflicts to the user, use ConflictsList for coloring rows.
   570	        /// </summary>
   571	        public IEnumerable<string> ConflictDescriptions
   572	            => conflicts.Where(kvp => kvp.Value == null
   573	                                      // Pick the pair with the least distantly selected one first
   574	                                      || totalDependers(kvp.Key) <= totalDependers(kvp.Value))
   575	                        .Select(kvp => string.Format(
   576	                            Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictsWith,
   577	                            conflictingModDescription(kvp.Key,   null),
   578	                            conflictingModDescription(kvp.Value, null)));
   579	
   580	        public bool IsConsistent => conflicts.Count == 0;
   581	
   582	        public List<SelectionReason> ReasonsFor(CkanModule mod)
   583	            => reasons.TryGetValue(mod, out List<SelectionReason>? r)
   584	                ? r
   585	                : new List<SelectionReason>();
   586	
   587	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> UserReasonsFor(CkanModule mod)
   588	            => allDependers(mod).Intersect(user_requested_mods);
   589	
   590	        /// <summary>
   591	        /// Indicates whether a module should be considered auto-installed in this change set.
   592	        /// A mod is auto-installed if it is in the list because it's a dependency
   593	        /// and if its depending mod is not a metpaackage.
   594	        /// </summary>
   595	        /// <param name="mod">Module to check</param>
   596	        /// <returns>
   597	        /// true if auto-installed, false otherwise
   598	        /// </returns>
   599	        public bool IsAutoInstalled(CkanModule mod)
   600	            => ReasonsFor(mod).All(reason => reason is SelectionReason.Depends dep
   601	                                             && dep.Parent != null
   602	                                             && !dep.Parent.IsMetapackage);
   603	
   604	        private void AddReason(CkanModule module, SelectionReason reason)
   605	        {
   606	            if (reasons.TryGetValue(module, out List<SelectionReason>? modReasons))
   607	            {
   608	                modReasons.Add(reason);
   609	            }
   610	            else
   611	            {
   612	                reasons.Add(module, new List<SelectionReason>() { reason });
   613	            }
   614	        }
   615	
   616	        private readonly ResolvedRelationshipsTree resolved;
   617	
   618	        /// <summary>
   619	        /// The list of all additional mods that need to be installed to satisfy all relationships.
   620	        /// </summary>
   621	        private readonly Dictionary<string, CkanModule> modlist = new Dictionary<string, CkanModule>();
   622	        private readonly List<CkanModule> user_requested_mods = new List<CkanModule>();
   623	
   624	        private readonly List<ModPair> conflicts = new List<ModPair>();
   625	        private readonly Dictionary<CkanModule, List<SelectionReason>> reasons =
   626	            new Dictionary<CkanModule, List<SelectionReason>>();
   627	
   628	        private readonly HashSet<string> dlls;
   629	
   630	        /// <summary>
   631	        /// Depends relationships with suppress_recommendations=true,
   632	        /// to be applied to all recommendations and suggestions
   633	        /// </summary>
   634	        private readonly HashSet<RelationshipDescriptor> suppressedRecommenders = new HashSet<RelationshipDescriptor>();
   635	
   636	        private readonly IRegistryQuerier            registry;
   637	        private readonly IGame                       game;
   638	        private readonly GameVersionCriteria         versionCrit;
   639	        private readonly RelationshipResolverOptions options;
   640	
   641	        /// <summary>
   642	        /// The list of already installed modules.
   643	        /// </summary>
   644	        private readonly HashSet<CkanModule> installed_modules;
   645	
   646	        private readonly HashSet<CkanModule> alreadyResolved = new HashSet<CkanModule>();
   647	
   648	        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(RelationshipResolver));
   649	    }
   650	
   651	}



2026-05-29 15:11:25,123 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - ========================= STEP 9 =========================
2026-05-29 15:11:25,126 - DEBUG - swea-lm-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - n_cache_control: 2
2026-05-29 15:11:35,477 - DEBUG - swea-lm-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - Response: ModelResponse(id='6cf9f134c07747e59fe5ff3208c6f6fa', created=1780067486, model='DeepSeek-V4-Pro', object='chat.completion', system_fingerprint=None, choices=[Choices(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, message=Message(content='Now let\'s look at the `ResolveStanza` method more carefully. The issue is about conflicts in recommends/suggests stanzas. When there\'s a conflict between recommended mods, some are hidden.\n\nLet me look at the key section in `ResolveStanza` - particularly lines 343-372 where conflicts are handled:\n\nThe issue is in lines 362-365: when `soft_resolve` is true (which it is for recommends/suggests) and there\'s a conflict, the code just logs "would cause conflicts, excluding it from consideration" and continues. But the problem is that it doesn\'t add the conflicting mod to the list at all. \n\nBut wait, the PR description says: "Having a \'recommends\' or a \'suggests\' stanza in the ckan will cause any mods which are listed as a conflict in an earlier line to hide the later ones."\n\nSo the issue is that if mod A and mod B both conflict with each other, and A appears first in the list, when B is processed, A is already in `modlist` and `fixed_mods`, so B is seen as conflicting with A and gets excluded. Then later mods (C, D, E) might also be affected.\n\nBut the expected behavior (from the PR) is: "I would have expected all the mods to be listed, and if two selected which have a conflict, to show them in red"\n\nSo the fix should be: for soft_resolve (recommends/suggests), when there\'s a conflict, instead of just skipping the conflicting module entirely, we should still add it but record the conflict.\n\nLet me look at how the non-soft-resolve case works with `proceed_with_inconsistencies`:\n\nIn lines 356-361:\n```csharp\nelse if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)\n{\n    Add(candidate, reason);\n    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(conflicting_mod, candidate));\n    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(candidate, conflicting_mod));\n}\n```\n\nSo for hard dependencies with `proceed_with_inconsistencies`, we add the module AND record the conflict. 2026-05-29 15:11:35,484 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let's look at the `ResolveStanza` method more carefully. The issue is about conflicts in recommends/suggests stanzas. When there's a conflict between recommended mods, some are hidden.

Let me look at the key section in `ResolveStanza` - particularly lines 343-372 where conflicts are handled:

The issue is in lines 362-365: when `soft_resolve` is true (which it is for recommends/suggests) and there's a conflict, the code just logs "would cause conflicts, excluding it from consideration" and continues. But the problem is that it doesn't add the conflicting mod to the list at all. 

But wait, the PR description says: "Having a 'recommends' or a 'suggests' stanza in the ckan will cause any mods which are listed as a conflict in an earlier line to hide the later ones."

So the issue is that if mod A and mod B both conflict with each other, and A appears first in the list, when B is processed, A is already in `modlist` and `fixed_mods`, so B is seen as conflicting with A and gets excluded. Then later mods (C, D, E) might also be affected.

But the expected behavior (from the PR) is: "I would have expected all the mods to be listed, and if two selected which have a conflict, to show them in red"

So the fix should be: for soft_resolve (recommends/suggests), when there's a conflict, instead of just skipping the conflicting module entirely, we should still add it but record the conflict.

Let me look at how the non-soft-resolve case works with `proceed_with_inconsistencies`:

In lines 356-361:
```csharp
else if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
{
    Add(candidate, reason);
    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(conflicting_mod, candidate));
    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(candidate, conflicting_mod));
}
```

So for hard dependencies with `proceed_with_inconsistencies`, we add the module AND record the conflict. But for soft_resolve (recommends/suggests), we just skip it entirely.

The fix should make the soft_resolve case behave similarly: add the module and record the conflict, rather than skipping it.

     5	    // TODO: It would be lovely to get rid of the `without` fields,

     8	    public class RelationshipResolverOptions
     9	    {
    10	        public RelationshipResolverOptions(StabilityToleranceConfig stabTolCfg)
    11	        {
    12	            stability_tolerance = stabTolCfg;
    13	        }
    14	
    15	        /// <summary>
    16	        /// Default options for relationship resolution.
    17	        /// </summary>
    18	        public static RelationshipResolverOptions DefaultOpts(StabilityToleranceConfig stabTolCfg)
    19	            => new RelationshipResolverOptions(stabTolCfg);
    20	
    21	        /// <summary>
    22	        /// Options to install without recommendations.
    23	        /// </summary>
    24	        public static RelationshipResolverOptions DependsOnlyOpts(StabilityToleranceConfig stabTolCfg)
    25	            => new RelationshipResolverOptions(stabTolCfg)
    26	            {
    27	                with_recommends   = false,
    28	                with_suggests     = false,
    29	                with_all_suggests = false,
    30	            };
    31	
    32	        /// <summary>
    33	        /// Options to find all dependencies, recommendations, and suggestions
    34	        /// of anything in the changeset (except when suppress_recommendations==true),
    35	        /// without throwing exceptions, so the calling code can decide what to do about conflicts
    36	        /// </summary>
    37	        public static RelationshipResolverOptions KitchenSinkOpts(StabilityToleranceConfig stabTolCfg)
    38	            => new RelationshipResolverOptions(stabTolCfg)
    39	            {
    40	                with_recommends                = true,
    41	                with_suggests                  = true,
    42	                without_toomanyprovides_kraken = true,
    43	                without_enforce_consistency    = true,
    44	                proceed_with_inconsistencies   = true,
    45	                get_recommenders               = true,
    46	            };
    47	
    48	        public static RelationshipResolverOptions ConflictsOpts(StabilityToleranceConfig stabTolCfg)
    49	            => new RelationshipResolverOptions(stabTolCfg)
    50	            {
    51	                without_toomanyprovides_kraken = true,
    52	                proceed_with_inconsistencies   = true,
    53	                without_enforce_consistency    = true,
    54	                with_recommends                = false,
    55	            };
    56	
    57	        /// <summary>
    58	        /// If true, add recommended mods, and their recommendations.
    59	        /// </summary>
    60	        public bool with_recommends = true;
    61	
    62	        /// <summary>
    63	        /// If true, add suggests, but not suggested suggests. :)
    64	        /// </summary>
    65	        public bool with_suggests = false;
    66	
    67	        /// <summary>
    68	        /// If true, add suggested modules, and *their* suggested modules, too!
    69	        /// </summary>
    70	        public bool with_all_suggests = false;
    71	
    72	        /// <summary>
    73	        /// If true, surpresses the TooManyProvides kraken when resolving
    74	        /// relationships. Otherwise, we just pick the first.
    75	        /// </summary>
    76	        public bool without_toomanyprovides_kraken = false;
    77	
    78	        /// <summary>
    79	        /// If true, we skip our sanity check at the end of our relationship
    80	        /// resolution. Note that non-sane resolutions can't actually be
    81	        /// installed, so this is mostly useful for giving the user feedback
    82	        /// on failed resolutions.
    83	        /// </summary>
    84	        public bool without_enforce_consistency = false;
    85	
    86	        /// <summary>
    87	        /// If true, we'll populate the `conflicts` field, rather than immediately
    88	        /// throwing a kraken when inconsistencies are detected. Again, these
    89	        /// solutions are non-installable, so mostly of use to provide user
    90	        /// feedback when things go wrong.
    91	        /// </summary>
    92	        public bool proceed_with_inconsistencies = false;
    93	
    94	        /// <summary>
    95	        /// If true, then if a module has no versions that are compatible with
    96	        /// the current game version, then we will consider incompatible versions
    97	        /// of that module.
    98	        /// This replaces the former behavior of ignoring compatibility for
    99	        /// `install identifier=version` commands.
   100	        /// </summary>
   101	        public bool allow_incompatible = false;
   102	
   103	        /// <summary>
   104	        /// If true, get the list of mods that should be checked for
   105	        /// recommendations and suggestions.
   106	        /// Differs from normal resolution in that it stops when
   107	        /// ModuleRelationshipDescriptor.suppress_recommendations==true
   108	        /// </summary>
   109	        public bool get_recommenders = false;
   110	
   111	        /// <summary>
   112	        /// The least stable category of mods to allow
   113	        /// </summary>
   114	        public StabilityToleranceConfig? stability_tolerance;
   115	
   116	        public RelationshipResolverOptions OptionsFor(RelationshipDescriptor descr)
   117	            => descr.suppress_recommendations ? WithoutRecommendations() : this;
   118	
   119	        public RelationshipResolverOptions WithoutRecommendations()
   120	        {
   121	            if (with_recommends || with_all_suggests || with_suggests)
   122	            {
   123	                var newOptions = (RelationshipResolverOptions)MemberwiseClone();
   124	                newOptions.with_recommends   = false;
   125	                newOptions.with_all_suggests = false;
   126	                newOptions.with_suggests     = false;
   127	                return newOptions;
   128	            }
   129	            return this;
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        public RelationshipResolverOptions WithoutSuggestions()
   133	        {
   134	            if (with_suggests)
   135	            {
   136	                var newOptions = (RelationshipResolverOptions)MemberwiseClone();
   137	                newOptions.with_suggests = false;
   138	                return newOptions;
   139	            }
   140	            return this;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        public OptionalRelationships OptionalHandling()
   144	            => (with_all_suggests ? OptionalRelationships.AllSuggestions | OptionalRelationships.Suggestions
   145	                                  : OptionalRelationships.None)
   146	               | (with_suggests   ? OptionalRelationships.Suggestions
   147	                                  : OptionalRelationships.None)
   148	               | (with_recommends ? OptionalRelationships.Recommendations
   149	                                  : OptionalRelationships.None);
   150	
   151	    }

   345	        [Test]
   346	        public void ModList_WithInstalledModules_ContainsThemWithReasonInstalled()
   347	        {
   348	            var user = new NullUser();
   349	            var mod_a = generator!.GenerateRandomModule();
   350	            using (var ksp = new DisposableKSP())
   351	            using (var repo = new TemporaryRepository(mod_a.ToJson()))
   352	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
   353	            {
   354	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
   355	                var list = new List<CkanModule> { mod_a };
   356	
   357	                registry.RegisterModule(mod_a, new List<string>(), ksp.KSP, false);
   358	
   359	                var relationship_resolver = new RelationshipResolver(
   360	                    list, null, options!, registry, game, crit);
   361	                CollectionAssert.Contains(relationship_resolver.ModList(), mod_a);
   362	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(new List<SelectionReason>
   363	                                          {
   364	                                              new SelectionReason.Installed(),
   365	                                              new SelectionReason.UserRequested(),
   366	                                          },
   367	                                          relationship_resolver.ReasonsFor(mod_a));
   368	            }
   369	        }

   478	                suggests: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
   479	                {
   480	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = suggested2.identifier }
   481	                }
   482	            );
   483	            var suggester = generator.GenerateRandomModule(
   484	                suggests: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
   485	                {
   486	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = suggested.identifier }
   487	                }
   488	            );
   489

   492	                                                      suggested.ToJson(),

   682	        [Test]

   685	        [TestCase("1.0", "1.0", "0.5")]//what to do if a mod is present twice with the same version ?
   686	        public void Constructor_WithDependentVersion_ChooseCorrectly(string ver, string dep, string other)
   687	        {
   688	            var dependent = generator!.GenerateRandomModule(version: new ModuleVersion(ver));
   689	            var other_dependent = generator.GenerateRandomModule(identifier: dependent.identifier, version: new ModuleVersion(other));
   690	
   691	            var depender = generator.GenerateRandomModule(depends: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
   692	            {
   693	                new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor
   694	                {
   695	                    name = dependent.identifier,
   696	                    version = new ModuleVersion(dep)
   697	                }
   698	            });
   699	
   700	            var user = new NullUser();

   702	                                                      dependent.ToJson(),
   703	                                                      other_dependent.ToJson()))
   704	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
   705	            {
   706	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
   707	                var list = new List<CkanModule> { depender };
   708	
   709	                var relationship_resolver = new RelationshipResolver(list, null, options!, registry, game, crit);
   710	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(relationship_resolver.ModList(), new List<CkanModule>
   711	                {
   712	                    dependent,
   713	                    depender
   714	                });
   715	            }
   716	        }

   797	        public void Constructor_WithDependentVersionMinMax_ChooseCorrectly(string ver, string dep_min, string dep_max, string other)
   798	        {
   799	            var dependent = generator!.GenerateRandomModule(version: new ModuleVersion(ver));
   800	            var other_dependent = generator.GenerateRandomModule(identifier: dependent.identifier, version: new ModuleVersion(other));

   803	            {

   814	                                                      dependent.ToJson(),
   815	                                                      other_dependent.ToJson()))
   816	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
   817	            {
   818	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
   819	                var list = new List<CkanModule> { depender };
   820	
   821	                var relationship_resolver = new RelationshipResolver(list, null, options!, registry, game, crit);
   822	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(relationship_resolver.ModList(), new List<CkanModule>
   823	                {
   824	                    dependent,
   825	                    depender
   826	                });
   827	            }
   828	        }

   874	        [Test]
   875	        public void Constructor_ReverseDependencyDoesntMatchLatest_ChoosesOlderVersion()
   876	        {
   877	            // Arrange
   878	            CkanModule depender = CkanModule.FromJson(@"{
   879	                ""spec_version"": 1,
   880	                ""identifier"":   ""depender"",
   881	                ""author"":       ""modder"",
   882	                ""version"":      ""1.0"",
   883	                ""download"":     ""https://kerbalstuff.com/mod/269/Dogecoin%20Flag/download/1.01"",
   884	                ""depends"": [ { ""name"": ""dependency"" } ]
   885	            }");
   886	
   887	            CkanModule olderDependency = CkanModule.FromJson(@"{
   888	                ""spec_version"": 1,
   889	                ""identifier"":   ""dependency"",
   890	                ""author"":       ""modder"",
   891	                ""version"":      ""1.0"",
   892	                ""download"":     ""https://kerbalstuff.com/mod/269/Dogecoin%20Flag/download/1.01"",
   893	                ""depends"": [ {
   894	                    ""name"":        ""depender"",
   895	                    ""min_version"": ""1.0""
   896	                } ]
   897	            }");
   898	
   899	            CkanModule newerDependency = CkanModule.FromJson(@"{
   900	                ""spec_version"": 1,
   901	                ""identifier"":   ""dependency"",
   902	                ""author"":       ""modder"",
   903	                ""version"":      ""2.0"",
   904	                ""download"":     ""https://kerbalstuff.com/mod/269/Dogecoin%20Flag/download/1.01"",
   905	                ""depends"": [ {
   906	                    ""name"":        ""depender"",
   907	                    ""min_version"": ""2.0""
   908	                } ]
   909	            }");
   910	
   911	            var user = new NullUser();
   912	            using (var repo = new TemporaryRepository(depender.ToJson(),
   913	                                                      olderDependency.ToJson(),
   914	                                                      newerDependency.ToJson()))
   915	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
   916	            {
   917	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
   918	
   919	                // Act
   920	                RelationshipResolver rr = new RelationshipResolver(
   921	                    new CkanModule[] { depender }, null,
   922	                    options!, registry, game, crit);
   923	
   924	                // Assert
   925	                CollectionAssert.Contains(      rr.ModList(), olderDependency);
   926	                CollectionAssert.DoesNotContain(rr.ModList(), newerDependency);
   927	            }
   928	        }

   944	                ""spec_version"": 1,
   945	                ""identifier"": ""dependency"",

   947	                ""version"":    ""1.0"",

   956	                ""download"":   ""https://kerbalstuff.com/mod/269/Dogecoin%20Flag/download/1.01"",
   957	                ""conflicts"": [ {

   960	            }");
   961	
   962	            var user = new NullUser();

   977	                CollectionAssert.DoesNotContain(rr.ModList(), newerDependency);
   978	            }

  1018	        [Test]
  1019	        public void ReasonFor_WithSuggestedMods_GivesCorrectParent()
  1020	        {
  1021	            var suggested = generator!.GenerateRandomModule();
  1022	            var mod = generator.GenerateRandomModule(suggests:
  1023	                new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1024	                {
  1025	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor
  1026	                    {
  1027	                        name = suggested.identifier
  1028	                    }
  1029	                });
  1030	
  1031	            var user = new NullUser();
  1032	            using (var repo = new TemporaryRepository(mod.ToJson(),
  1033	                                                      suggested.ToJson()))
  1034	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1035	            {
  1036	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1037	                var list = new List<CkanModule> { mod };
  1038	
  1039	                options!.with_all_suggests = true;
  1040	                var relationship_resolver = new RelationshipResolver(list, null, options, registry, game, crit);
  1041	                var reasons = relationship_resolver.ReasonsFor(suggested);
  1042	
  1043	                Assert.IsTrue(reasons[0] is SelectionReason.Suggested sug
  1044	                              && sug.Parent == mod);
  1045	            }
  1046	        }

  1048	        [Test]
  1049	        public void ReasonFor_WithTreeOfMods_GivesCorrectParents()
  1050	        {
  1051	            var suggested = generator!.GenerateRandomModule();
  1052	            var recommendedA = generator.GenerateRandomModule();
  1053	            var recommendedB = generator.GenerateRandomModule();
  1054	            var mod = generator.GenerateRandomModule(
  1055	                suggests: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1056	                {
  1057	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = suggested.identifier }
  1058	                }
  1059	            );
  1060	            suggested.recommends = new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1061	            {
  1062	                new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = recommendedA.identifier },
  1063	                new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = recommendedB.identifier }
  1064	            };
  1065	
  1066	            var user = new NullUser();
  1067	            using (var repo = new TemporaryRepository(mod.ToJson(),
  1068	                                                      suggested.ToJson(),
  1069	                                                      recommendedA.ToJson(),
  1070	                                                      recommendedB.ToJson()))
  1071	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1072	            {
  1073	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1074	                var list = new List<CkanModule> { mod };
  1075	
  1076	                options!.with_all_suggests = true;
  1077	                options.with_recommends = true;
  1078	                var relationship_resolver = new RelationshipResolver(list, null, options, registry, game, crit);
  1079	                var reasons = relationship_resolver.ReasonsFor(recommendedA);
  1080	                Assert.IsTrue(reasons[0] is SelectionReason.Recommended rec
  1081	                              && rec.Parent.Equals(suggested));
  1082	                reasons = relationship_resolver.ReasonsFor(recommendedB);
  1083	                Assert.IsTrue(reasons[0] is SelectionReason.Recommended rec2
  1084	                              && rec2.Parent.Equals(suggested));
  1085	            }
  1086	        }

  1088	        // The whole point of autodetected mods is they can participate in relationships.
  1089	        // This makes sure they can (at least for dependencies). It may overlap with other
  1090	        // tests, but that's cool, beacuse it's a test. :D
  1091	        [Test]
  1092	        public void AutodetectedCanSatisfyRelationships()
  1093	        {
  1094	            var user = new NullUser();
  1095	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user))
  1096	            using (var ksp = new DisposableKSP())

  1100	                {

  1104	                                                               "ModuleManager.dll"))
  1105	                    }

  1107	
  1108	                var depends = new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1109	                {
  1110	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor { name = "ModuleManager" }
  1111	                };

  1113	                CkanModule mod = generator!.GenerateRandomModule(depends: depends);
  1114	
  1115	                new RelationshipResolver(
  1116	                    new CkanModule[] { mod }, null, RelationshipResolverOptions.DefaultOpts(stabilityTolerance),
  1117	                    registry, game, new GameVersionCriteria(GameVersion.Parse("1.0.0")));
  1118	            }
  1119	        }

  1121	        [Test,
  1122	         TestCase(new string[] {
  1123	                      @"{
  1124	                          ""identifier"": ""Deferred"",
  1125	                          ""conflicts"": [
  1126	                              {
  1127	                                  ""name"":        ""RasterPropMonitor"",
  1128	                                  ""max_version"": ""1:v0.31.13.4""
  1129	                              }
  1130	                          ]
  1131	                      }",
  1132	                      @"{
  1133	                          ""identifier"": ""RasterPropMonitor"",
  1134	                          ""version"":    ""1:v1.0.2""
  1135	                      }",
  1136	                  },
  1137	                  new string[] { "Deferred", "RasterPropMonitor" })]
  1138	        public void Constructor_UpgradeVersionSpecificConflictedAutoDetected_DoesNotThrow(
  1139	                string[] availableModules,
  1140	                string[] installIdents)
  1141	        {
  1142	            var user = new NullUser();
  1143	            var crit = new GameVersionCriteria(new GameVersion(1, 12, 5));
  1144	            using (var repo     = new TemporaryRepository(availableModules.Select(MergeWithDefaults)
  1145	                                                                          .ToArray()))
  1146	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1147	            using (var inst     = new DisposableKSP())
  1148	            {
  1149	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1150	                registry.SetDlls(new Dictionary<string, string>()
  1151	                {
  1152	                    {
  1153	                        "RasterPropMonitor",
  1154	                        inst.KSP.ToRelativeGameDir(Path.Combine(inst.KSP.Game.PrimaryModDirectory(inst.KSP),
  1155	                                                               "RasterPropMonitor.dll"))
  1156	                    }
  1157	                });
  1158	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(() =>
  1159	                {
  1160	                    var rr = new RelationshipResolver(
  1161	                        installIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit))
  1162	                                     .OfType<CkanModule>(),
  1163	                        null,
  1164	                        RelationshipResolverOptions.DependsOnlyOpts(stabilityTolerance),
  1165	                        registry, inst.KSP.Game, crit);
  1166	                });
  1167	            }
  1168	        }
  1169	
  1170	        // Models the EVE - EVE-Config - AVP - AVP-Textures relationship
  1171	        [Test]
  1172	        public void UninstallingConflictingModule_InstallingRecursiveDependencies_ResolvesSuccessfully()
  1173	        {
  1174	            // Arrange: create dummy modules that resemble the relationship entanglement, and make them available
  1175	            var eve = generator!.GenerateRandomModule(
  1176	                identifier: "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements",
  1177	                depends: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1178	                    {new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config"}}
  1179	            );
  1180	            var eveDefaultConfig = generator.GenerateRandomModule(
  1181	                identifier: "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config-stock",
  1182	                provides: new List<string> {"EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config"},
  1183	                conflicts: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1184	                    {new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config"}}
  1185	            );
  1186	            var avp = generator.GenerateRandomModule(
  1187	                identifier: "AstronomersVisualPack",
  1188	                provides: new List<string> {"EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config"},
  1189	                depends: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1190	                {
  1191	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "AVP-Textures"},
  1192	                    new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements"}
  1193	                },
  1194	                conflicts: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1195	                        {new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "EnvironmentalVisualEnhancements-Config"}}
  1196	            );
  1197	            var avp2kTextures = generator.GenerateRandomModule(
  1198	                identifier: "AVP-2kTextures",
  1199	                provides: new List<string> {"AVP-Textures"},
  1200	                depends: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1201	                    {new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "AstronomersVisualPack"}},
  1202	                conflicts: new List<RelationshipDescriptor>
  1203	                    {new ModuleRelationshipDescriptor {name = "AVP-Textures"}}
  1204	            );
  1205	            var user = new NullUser();
  1206	            using (var ksp = new DisposableKSP())
  1207	            using (var repo = new TemporaryRepository(eve.ToJson(),
  1208	                                                      eveDefaultConfig.ToJson(),
  1209	                                                      avp.ToJson(),
  1210	                                                      avp2kTextures.ToJson()))
  1211	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1212	            {
  1213	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1214	
  1215	                // Start with eve and eveDefaultConfig installed
  1216	                registry.RegisterModule(eve, new List<string>(), ksp.KSP, false);
  1217	                registry.RegisterModule(eveDefaultConfig, new List<string>(), ksp.KSP, false);
  1218	
  1219	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(registry.CheckSanity);
  1220	
  1221	                List<CkanModule> modulesToInstall;
  1222	                List<CkanModule> modulesToRemove;
  1223	                RelationshipResolver? resolver;
  1224	
  1225	                // Act and assert: play through different possible user interactions
  1226	                // Scenario 1 - Try installing AVP, expect an exception for proceed_with_inconsistencies=false
  1227	
  1228	                modulesToInstall = new List<CkanModule> { avp };
  1229	                modulesToRemove = new List<CkanModule>();
  1230	
  1231	                options!.proceed_with_inconsistencies = false;
  1232	                var exception = Assert.Throws<InconsistentKraken>(() =>
  1233	                {
  1234	                    resolver = new RelationshipResolver(modulesToInstall, modulesToRemove, options, registry, game, crit);
  1235	                });
  1236	                Assert.AreEqual($"{avp} conflicts with {eveDefaultConfig}",
  1237	                                exception?.ShortDescription);
  1238	
  1239	                // Scenario 2 - Try installing AVP, expect no exception for proceed_with_inconsistencies=true, but a conflict list
  1240	
  1241	                resolver = null;
  1242	                options.proceed_with_inconsistencies = true;
  1243	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(() =>
  1244	                {
  1245	                    resolver = new RelationshipResolver(modulesToInstall, modulesToRemove, options, registry, game, crit);
  1246	                });
  1247	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(modulesToInstall,
  1248	                                               resolver?.ConflictList.Keys);
  1249	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(new List<string> {$"{avp} conflicts with {eveDefaultConfig}"},
  1250	                                               resolver?.ConflictList.Values);
  1251	
  1252	                // Scenario 3 - Try uninstalling eveDefaultConfig and installing avp, should work and result in no conflicts
  1253	
  1254	                modulesToInstall = new List<CkanModule> { avp };
  1255	                modulesToRemove = new List<CkanModule> { eveDefaultConfig };
  1256	
  1257	                resolver = null;
  1258	                options.proceed_with_inconsistencies = false;
  1259	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(() =>
  1260	                {
  1261	                    resolver = new RelationshipResolver(modulesToInstall, modulesToRemove, options, registry, game, crit);
  1262	                });
  1263	                Assert.IsEmpty(resolver!.ConflictList);
  1264	                CollectionAssert.AreEquivalent(new List<CkanModule> {avp, avp2kTextures}, resolver.ModList());
  1265	            }
  1266	        }
  1267	
  1268	        [Test,
  1269	         TestCase(new string[] {
  1270	                      @"{
  1271	                          ""identifier"": ""MyDLC"",
  1272	                          ""kind"": ""dlc""
  1273	                      }",
  1274	                      @"{
  1275	                          ""identifier"": ""InstallingMod"",
  1276	                          ""recommends"": [ { ""name"": ""MyDLC"" } ]
  1277	                      }",
  1278	                  },
  1279	                  new string[] { "InstallingMod" },
  1280	                  new string[] { "MyDLC" }),
  1281	        ]
  1282	        public void Recommendations_WithDLCRecommendationUnsatisfied_ContainsDLC(string[] availableModules,
  1283	                                                                                 string[] installIdents,
  1284	                                                                                 string[] dlcIdents)
  1285	        {
  1286	            // Arrange
  1287	            var user    = new NullUser();
  1288	            var game    = new KerbalSpaceProgram();
  1289	            var crit    = new GameVersionCriteria(new GameVersion(1, 12, 5));
  1290	            using (var repo     = new TemporaryRepository(availableModules.Select(MergeWithDefaults)
  1291	                                                                          .ToArray()))
  1292	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1293	            {
  1294	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1295	
  1296	                // Act
  1297	                var rr = new RelationshipResolver(
  1298	                    installIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit))
  1299	                                 .OfType<CkanModule>(),
  1300	                    null,
  1301	                    RelationshipResolverOptions.KitchenSinkOpts(stabilityTolerance),
  1302	                    registry, game, crit);
  1303	                var deps = rr.Dependencies().ToHashSet();
  1304	                var recs = rr.Recommendations(deps).ToArray();
  1305	                var dlcs = dlcIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit)).ToArray();
  1306	
  1307	                // Assert
  1308	                CollectionAssert.IsSubsetOf(dlcs, rr.ModList(false));
  1309	                CollectionAssert.IsSubsetOf(dlcs, recs);
  1310	            }
  1311	        }
  1312	
  1313	        [Test,
  1314	         TestCase(new string[] {
  1315	                      @"{
  1316	                          ""identifier"": ""MyDLC"",
  1317	                          ""kind"": ""dlc""
  1318	                      }",
  1319	                      @"{
  1320	                          ""identifier"": ""InstallingMod"",
  1321	                          ""recommends"": [ { ""name"": ""MyDLC"" } ]
  1322	                      }",
  1323	                  },
  1324	                  new string[] { "InstallingMod" },
  1325	                  new string[] { "MyDLC" }),
  1326	        ]
  1327	        public void Recommendations_WithDLCRecommendationSatisfied_OmitsDLC(string[] availableModules,
  1328	                                                                            string[] installIdents,
  1329	                                                                            string[] dlcIdents)
  1330	        {
  1331	            // Arrange
  1332	            var user    = new NullUser();
  1333	            var game    = new KerbalSpaceProgram();
  1334	            var crit    = new GameVersionCriteria(new GameVersion(1, 12, 5));
  1335	            using (var repo     = new TemporaryRepository(availableModules.Select(MergeWithDefaults)
  1336	                                                                          .ToArray()))
  1337	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1338	            {
  1339	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1340	                registry.SetDlcs(dlcIdents.ToDictionary(ident => ident,
  1341	                                                        ident => new UnmanagedModuleVersion("1.0.0")));
  1342	
  1343	                // Act
  1344	                var rr = new RelationshipResolver(
  1345	                    installIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit))
  1346	                                 .OfType<CkanModule>(),
  1347	                    null,
  1348	                    RelationshipResolverOptions.KitchenSinkOpts(stabilityTolerance),
  1349	                    registry, game, crit);
  1350	                var deps = rr.Dependencies().ToHashSet();
  1351	                var recs = rr.Recommendations(deps).ToArray();
  1352	
  1353	                // Assert
  1354	                foreach (var mod in dlcIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit)))
  1355	                {
  1356	                    CollectionAssert.DoesNotContain(rr.ModList(false), mod);
  1357	                    CollectionAssert.DoesNotContain(recs,              mod);
  1358	                }
  1359	            }
  1360	        }
