  1593	        public void Constructor_WithPlayModes_DoesNotThrow(string[] availableModules,
  1594	                                                           string[] installIdents,
  1595	                                                           string[] goodSubstrings,
  1596	                                                           string[] badSubstrings)
  1597	        {
  1598	            // Arrange
  1599	            var user = new NullUser();
  1600	            var crit = new GameVersionCriteria(new GameVersion(1, 12, 5));
  1601	            using (var repo     = new TemporaryRepository(availableModules.Select(MergeWithDefaults)
  1602	                                                                          .ToArray()))
  1603	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1604	            {
  1605	                var registry = new CKAN.Registry(repoData.Manager, repo.repo);
  1606	
  1607	                // Act / Assert
  1608	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(() =>
  1609	                {
  1610	                    var rr = new RelationshipResolver(
  1611	                        installIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident, stabilityTolerance, crit))
  1612	                                     .OfType<CkanModule>(),
  1613	                        null,
  1614	                        RelationshipResolverOptions.DependsOnlyOpts(stabilityTolerance),
  1615	                        registry, game, crit);
  1616	                    var idents = rr.ModList().Select(m => m.identifier).ToArray();
  1617	                    foreach (var goodSubstring in goodSubstrings)
  1618	                    {
  1619	                        Assert.IsTrue(idents.Any(ident => ident.Contains(goodSubstring)),
  1620	                                      $"Some identifier containing {goodSubstring} must be in resolver");
  1621	                    }
  1622	                    foreach (var ident in idents)
  1623	                    {
  1624	                        foreach (var badSubstring in badSubstrings)
  1625	                        {
  1626	                            Assert.IsFalse(ident.Contains(badSubstring),
  1627	                                           $"No identifiers containing {badSubstring} should be in resolver");
  1628	                        }
  1629	                    }
  1630	                });
  1631	            }
  1632	        }

  1830	        public void Constructor_DifferentVersionDepends_Throws(string[] availableModules,
  1831	                                                               string[] installIdents,
  1832	                                                               string[] errors)
  1833	        {
  1834	            // Arrange
  1835	            var user = new NullUser();
  1836	            using (var inst     = new DisposableKSP())
  1837	            using (var repo     = new TemporaryRepository(availableModules.Select(MergeWithDefaults)
  1838	                                                                          .ToArray()))
  1839	            using (var repoData = new TemporaryRepositoryData(user, repo.repo))
  1840	            using (var regMgr   = RegistryManager.Instance(inst.KSP, repoData.Manager,
  1841	                                                           new Repository[] { repo.repo }))
  1842	            {
  1843	                var registry  = regMgr.registry;
  1844	                var opts      = RelationshipResolverOptions.DefaultOpts(inst.KSP.StabilityToleranceConfig);
  1845	                var toInstall = installIdents.Select(ident => registry.LatestAvailable(ident,
  1846	                                                                  inst.KSP.StabilityToleranceConfig,
  1847	                                                                  inst.KSP.VersionCriteria()))
  1848	                                             .OfType<CkanModule>()
  1849	                                             .ToArray();
  1850	
  1851	                // Act / Assert
  1852	                var exc = Assert.Throws<DependenciesNotSatisfiedKraken>(() =>
  1853	                {
  1854	                    var sut = new RelationshipResolver(toInstall, Array.Empty<CkanModule>(), opts,
  1855	                                                       registry, inst.KSP.Game, inst.KSP.VersionCriteria());
  1856	                })!;
  1857	                CollectionAssert.AreEqual(errors, exc.Message.Split(new string[] { Environment.NewLine},
  1858	                                                                    StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries));
  1859	
  1860	                opts.proceed_with_inconsistencies = true;
  1861	                opts.without_enforce_consistency  = true;
  1862	                Assert.DoesNotThrow(() =>
  1863	                {
  1864	                    var sut = new RelationshipResolver(toInstall, Array.Empty<CkanModule>(), opts,
  1865	                                                       registry, inst.KSP.Game, inst.KSP.VersionCriteria());
  1866	                });
  1867	            }
  1868	        }

Now let me understand the issue better. Looking at the `ResolveStanza` method, lines 343-372:

```csharp
var conflicting_mod = fixed_mods.FirstOrDefault(mod => mod.ConflictsWith(candidate));
if (conflicting_mod == null)
{
    // Okay, looks like we want this one. Adding.
    Add(candidate, ...);
    Resolve(candidate, options, stanza);
}
else if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
{
    Add(candidate, reason);
    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(conflicting_mod, candidate));
    conflicts.Add(new ModPair(candidate, conflicting_mod));
}
else if (soft_resolve)
{
    log.InfoFormat("{0} would cause conflicts, excluding it from consideration", candidate);
}
else
{
    throw new InconsistentKraken(...);
}
```

The issue is that when `soft_resolve` is true (which it is for recommends and suggests), and there's a conflict, the module is simply excluded. But the PR says it should be included - all recommended/suggested mods should be listed, and if two selected have a conflict, they should be shown in red.

The fix should change the `soft_resolve` case to add the module and record the conflict, similar to the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` case. The difference is that for soft_resolve, we don't need `proceed_with_inconsistencies` to be set - we should always include conflicting recommended/suggested mods.

Good, we can run tests from the pre-built DLLs. Now let me look at the key issue more carefully.

The issue is in `ResolveStanza` at lines 343-372. When a recommended/suggested module has a conflict with something already in the list, it gets silently excluded (the `soft_resolve` branch). But according to the PR, we should still include it and mark the conflict.

Let me examine the logic flow more carefully:

1. In `AddModulesToInstall`, user-requested mods are added first (lines 89-114)
2. For each user-requested mod, `Resolve` is called (lines 119-123)
3. `Resolve` calls `ResolveStanza` for depends, then recommends, then suggests
4. In `ResolveStanza`, for each descriptor in the stanza:
   - If it matches something already in the changeset, add reason and resolve
   - If it matches something already installed, skip
   - Get candidates from registry
   - Check if candidate conflicts with anything in fixed_mods
   - If no conflict: add it
   - If conflict and proceed_with_inconsistencies: add it and record conflict
   - If conflict and soft_resolve: **skip it entirely** (THIS IS THE BUG)
   - Otherwise: throw

The bug is that when `soft_resolve` is true (recommends/suggests), conflicting mods are silently excluded. The fix should make them still be included but record the conflict, similar to the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` case.

Now, there's also another issue: even in the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` path for recommends/suggests, the code at line 362-365 is only reached if `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is false. Let me trace the logic:

For recommends/suggests, `soft_resolve` is true. If `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is also true, then the `else if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)` branch at line 356 is taken, which adds the mod and records the conflict. That's fine.

But if `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is false (the default), then we fall to `else if (soft_resolve)` at line 362, which silently excludes the mod. That's the problem.

The fix should change the behavior so that for soft_resolve (recommends/suggests), we add the module and record the conflict, similar to `proceed_with_inconsistencies`. The difference is that for hard dependencies (non-soft-resolve), we'd still throw.

Let me make the change

```csharp
if (options.with_recommends)
{
    ResolveStanza(module.recommends, new SelectionReason.Recommended(module, 0),
                  options.get_recommenders ? options.WithoutRecommendations()
                                           : options.WithoutSuggestions(),
                  true, old_stanza);
}

if (options.with_suggests || options.with_all_suggests)
{
    ResolveStanza(module.suggests, new SelectionReason.Suggested(module),
                  options.get_recommenders ? options.WithoutRecommendations()
                                           : options.WithoutSuggestions(),
                  true, old_stanza);
}
```

Both recommends and suggests are called with `soft_resolve = true`. So my change should affect both.

But wait, there's also an issue with `proceed_with_inconsistencies` for the initial user-requested modules. Looking at lines 94-110:

```csharp
var conflictingModules = modlist.Values
                                .Concat(installed_modules)
                                .Where(listed_mod => listed_mod.ConflictsWith(module));
foreach (CkanModule listed_mod in conflictingModules)
{
    if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
    {
        conflicts.Add(new ModPair(listed_mod, module));
        conflicts.Add(new ModPair(module, listed_mod));
    }
    else
    {
        throw new InconsistentKraken(...);
    }
}
```

This handles conflicts between user-requested modules. But what about conflicts between a recommended module and an already-added recommended module? That would go through `ResolveStanza` → the conflict check at line 343, which now with my fix will add both and record the conflict.

Now let me think about edge cases:
1. What if `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is true AND `soft_resolve` is true? The `proceed_with_inconsistencies` branch at line 356 would be taken first, so my change doesn't affect that path.
2. What if `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is false AND `soft_resolve` is true? My change now makes it add the module and record the conflict instead of silently excluding it.
3. What if both are false? That's for hard dependencies, and it still throws.

This looks correct.

   375	
   376	        private string conflictingModDescription(CkanModule? mod, CkanModule? parent)
   377	            => mod == null
   378	                ? Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverAnUnmanaged
   379	                : parent == null && ReasonsFor(mod).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.UserRequested
   380	                                                               or SelectionReason.Installed)
   381	                    // No parenthetical needed if it's user requested
   382	                    ? mod.ToString()
   383	                    // Explain why we're looking at this mod
   384	                    : string.Format(Properties.Resources.RelationshipResolverConflictingModDescription,
   385	                                    mod.ToString(),
   386	                                    string.Join(", ", UserReasonsFor(parent ?? mod).Select(m => m.ToString())));
   387	
   388	        /// <summary>
   389	        /// Adds the specified module to the list of modules we're installing.
   390	        /// This also adds its provides list to what we have available.
   391	        /// </summary>
   392	        private void Add(CkanModule module, SelectionReason reason)
   393	        {
   394	            log.DebugFormat("Adding {0} {1}", module.identifier, module.version);
   395	
   396	            if (modlist.TryGetValue(module.identifier, out CkanModule? possibleDup))
   397	            {
   398	                if (possibleDup.identifier == module.identifier)
   399	                {
   400	                    if (possibleDup.version == module.version
   401	                        && !possibleDup.MetadataEquals(module))
   402	                    {
   403	                        // If the version is the same and the metadata changed,
   404	                        // queue this up as a reinstall (remove the old version)
   405	                        reasons.Remove(possibleDup);
   406	                        modlist.Remove(possibleDup.identifier);
   407	                    }
   408	                    else
   409	                    {
   410	                        // We should never add the same module twice!
   411	                        log.ErrorFormat("Assertion failed: Already added {0}, can't add {1} ({2})",
   412	                                        possibleDup, module, reason);
   413	                        throw new ArgumentException($"Already added {possibleDup}, can't add {module} ({reason})");
   414	                    }
   415	                }
   416	                else
   417	                {
   418	                    // Duplicates via "provides" are OK though, we'll just replace it
   419	                    modlist.Remove(module.identifier);
   420	                }
   421	            }
   422	            modlist.Add(module.identifier, module);
   423	            AddReason(module, reason);
   424	
   425	            log.DebugFormat("Added {0}", module.identifier);
   426	            // Stop here if it doesn't have any provide aliases.
   427	            if (module.provides == null)
   428	            {
   429	                return;
   430	            }
   431	
   432	            // Handle provides/aliases if it does.
   433	
   434	            // It's okay if there's already a key for one of our aliases
   435	            // in the resolution list. In which case, we don't do anything.
   436	            var aliases = module.provides.Where(alias => !modlist.ContainsKey(alias));
   437	            foreach (string alias in aliases)
   438	            {
   439	                log.DebugFormat("Adding {0} providing {1}", module.identifier, alias);
   440	                modlist.Add(alias, module);
   441	            }
   442	        }
   443	
   444	        /// <summary>
   445	        /// Returns a list of all modules to install to satisfy the changes required.
   446	        /// Each mod is after its dependencies and before its reverse dependencies.
   447	        /// </summary>
   448	        public IEnumerable<CkanModule> ModList(bool parallel = true)
   449	            => modlist.Values.Distinct()
   450	                             .AsParallelIf(parallel)
   451	                             // Put user choices at the bottom; .OrderBy(bool) -> false first
   452	                             .OrderBy(m => ReasonsFor(m).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.UserRequested))
   453	                             // Put dependencies before dependers
   454	                             .ThenByDescending(totalDependers)
   455	                             // Resolve ties in name order
   456	                             .ThenBy(m => m.name);
   457	
   458	        public bool ReadyToInstall(CkanModule                      mod,
   459	                                   IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule> installed)
   460	            => !modlist.Values.Distinct()
   461	                              .Where(m => m != mod)
   462	                              .Except(installed)
   463	                              // Ignore circular dependencies
   464	                              .Except(allDependers(mod))
   465	                              .SelectMany(allDependers)
   466	                              .Contains(mod);
   467	
   468	        // The more nodes of the reverse-dependency graph we can paint, the higher up in the list it goes
   469	        private int totalDependers(CkanModule module)
   470	            => allDependers(module).Count();
   471	
   472	        private static IEnumerable<T> BreadthFirstSearch<T>(IEnumerable<T>                      startingGroup,
   473	                                                            Func<T, HashSet<T>, IEnumerable<T>> getNextGroup)
   474	        {
   475	            var found    = startingGroup.ToHashSet();
   476	            var toSearch = new Queue<T>(found);
   477	
   478	            while (toSearch.Count > 0)
   479	            {
   480	                var searching = toSearch.Dequeue();
   481	                yield return searching;
tail: write error: Broken pipe

So this is fine - user-requested modules always get added, and conflicts are recorded if `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is set, or an exception is thrown.

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **Conflict between a user-requested module and a recommended module**: The user-requested module is added first (in `AddModulesToInstall`). Then when resolving recommends, the recommended module is processed. Since the user-requested module is in `modlist`, the recommended module will be found conflicting at line 343. With my fix, it will be added and the conflict recorded.

2. **Conflict between two recommended mods**: The first recommended mod is added to `modlist`. When the second is processed, it conflicts with the first. With my fix, both are in `modlist` and the conflict is recorded.

3. **Conflict between a dependency and a recommended mod**: The dependency is added first (hard resolve). Then the recommended mod conflicts. With my fix, both are added and conflict recorded.

4. **Conflict between an already-installed mod and a recommended mod**: The installed mod is in `installed_modules`. The recommended mod conflicts with it. My fix adds it and records the conflict.

- The recommended mod might have its own dependencies that need to be pulled in
- The recommended mod might have its own recommendations that should be considered

Actually, I think the reason `proceed_with_inconsistencies` doesn't call `Resolve` is that when there's a conflict, the whole solution is already invalid, so there's no point in resolving further. But for recommends/suggests, we DO want to continue resolving even with conflicts, because the user should be able to see all recommendations and then decide which ones to pick.

Hmm, but looking at this more, I realize that adding `Resolve` here could cause issues. If a recommended mod conflicts with something, resolving its dependencies could pull in more mods that might also conflict, potentially causing a cascade. But actually, since `soft_resolve` is true for those recursive calls too, they'd just add more mods and record more conflicts.

However, I'll keep my change minimal and consistent with the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` behavior - just add the module and record the conflict without further resolution. The PR description doesn't mention anything about dependencies of conflicting recommended mods, it just says all recommended mods should be listed.

Let me now also check the `SanityChecker.EnforceConsistency` call at lines 127-137:

```csharp
try
{
    // Check that our solution is actually sane
    SanityChecker.EnforceConsistency(modlist.Values.Concat(installed_modules),
                                     dlls,
                                     registry.InstalledDlc);
}
catch (BadRelationshipsKraken k) when (options.without_enforce_consistency)
{
    conflicts.AddRange(k.Conflicts.Select(tuple => new ModPair(tuple.Item1, tuple.Item3))
                                  .Where(pair => !conflicts.Contains(pair))
                                  .ToArray());
}
```

This runs after all resolution is done. If `without_enforce_consistency` is set, it catches any additional conflicts and adds them to the list. This should still work with my change - any conflicts between the newly added recommended mods and other mods will be caught here too.

2026-05-29 15:18:42,542 - DEBUG - swea-tools-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - Retrieved state from environment: {}
2026-05-29 15:18:42,546 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

        public static bool FindRecommendations(GameInstance                                          instance,
                                               IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule>                       sourceModules,
                                               IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule>                       toInstall,
                                               IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule>                       toRemove,
                                               IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule>                       exclude,
                                               Registry                                              registry,
                                               out Dictionary<CkanModule, Tuple<bool, List<string>>> recommendations,
                                               out Dictionary<CkanModule, List<string>>              suggestions,
                                               out Dictionary<CkanModule, HashSet<string>>           supporters)
        {
            log.DebugFormat("Finding recommendations for: {0}", string.Join(", ", sourceModules));
            var crit     = instance.VersionCriteria();

            var rmvIdents = toRemove.Select(m => m.identifier).ToHashSet();
            var allRemoving = toRemove
                .Concat(registry.FindRemovableAutoInstalled(sourceModules, rmvIdents, instance)
                                .Select(im => im.Module))
                .ToArray();

            var resolver = new RelationshipResolver(sourceModules.Where(m => !m.IsDLC),
                                                    allRemoving,
                                                    RelationshipResolverOptions.KitchenSinkOpts(instance.StabilityToleranceConfig),
                                                    registry, instance.Game, crit);
            var recommenders = resolver.Dependencies().ToHashSet();
            log.DebugFormat("Recommenders: {0}", string.Join(", ", recommenders));

            var checkedRecs = resolver.Recommendations(recommenders)
                                      .Except(exclude)
                                      .Where(m => resolver.ReasonsFor(m)
                                                          .Any(r => r is SelectionReason.Recommended { ProvidesIndex: 0 }))
                                      .ToHashSet();
            var conflicting = new RelationshipResolver(toInstall.Concat(checkedRecs), allRemoving,
                                                       RelationshipResolverOptions.ConflictsOpts(instance.StabilityToleranceConfig),
                                                       registry, instance.Game, crit)
                                  .ConflictList.Keys;
            // Don't check recommendations that conflict with installed or installing mods
            checkedRecs.ExceptWith(conflicting);

            recommendations = resolver.Recommendations(recommenders)
                                      .Except(exclude)
                                      .ToDictionary(m => m,
                                                    m => new Tuple<bool, List<string>>(
                                                             checkedRecs.Contains(m),
                                                             resolver.ReasonsFor(m)
                                                                     .OfType<SelectionReason.Recommended>()
                                                                     .Where(r => recommenders.Contains(r.Parent))
                                                                     .Select(r => r.Parent)
                                                                     .OfType<CkanModule>()
                                                                     .Select(m => m.identifier)
                                                                     .ToList()));
            suggestions = resolver.Suggestions(recommenders,
                                               recommendations.Keys.ToList())
                                  .Except(exclude)
                                  .ToDictionary(m => m,
                                                m => resolver.ReasonsFor(m)
                                                             .OfType<SelectionReason.Suggested>()
                                                             .Where(r => recommenders.Contains(r.Parent))
                                                             .Select(r => r.Parent)
                                                             .OfType<CkanModule>()
                                                             .Select(m => m.identifier)
                                                             .ToList());

            var opts = RelationshipResolverOptions.DependsOnlyOpts(instance.StabilityToleranceConfig);
            supporters = resolver.Supporters(recommenders,
                                             recommenders.Concat(recommendations.Keys)
                                                         .Concat(suggestions.Keys))
                                 .Where(kvp => !exclude.Contains(kvp.Key)
                                               && CanInstall(toInstall.Append(kvp.Key).ToList(),
                                                          opts, registry, instance.Game, crit))
                                 .ToDictionary();

            return recommendations.Count > 0
                || suggestions.Count > 0
                || supporters.Count > 0;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Determine whether there is any way to install the given set of mods.
        /// Handles virtual dependencies, including recursively.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="opts">Installer options</param>
        /// <param name="toInstall">Mods we want to install</param>
        /// <param name="registry">Registry of instance into which we want to install</param>
        /// <param name="game">Game instance</param>
        /// <param name="crit">Game version criteria</param>
        /// <returns>
        /// True if it's possible to install these mods, false otherwise
        /// </returns>
        public static bool CanInstall(IReadOnlyCollection<CkanModule> toInstall,
                                      RelationshipResolverOptions     opts,
                                      IRegistryQuerier                registry,
                                      IGame                           game,
                                      GameVersionCriteria             crit)
        {
            string request = string.Join(", ", toInstall.Select(m => m.identifier));
            try
            {
                var installed = toInstall.Select(m => registry.InstalledModule(m.identifier)?.Module)
                                         .OfType<CkanModule>();
                var resolver = new RelationshipResolver(toInstall, installed, opts, registry, game, crit);

                var resolverModList = resolver.ModList(false).ToArray();
                if (resolverModList.Length >= toInstall.Count(m => !m.IsMetapackage))
                {
                    // We can install with no further dependencies
                    string recipe = string.Join(", ", resolverModList.Select(m => m.identifier));
                    log.Debug($"Installable: {request}: {recipe}");
                    return true;
                }
                else
                {
                    log.DebugFormat("Can't install {0}: {1}", request, string.Join("; ", resolver.ConflictDescriptions));
                    return false;
                }
            }
            catch (TooManyModsProvideKraken k)
            {
                // One of the dependencies is virtual
                foreach (var mod in k.modules)
                {
                    // Try each option recursively to see if any are successful
                    if (CanInstall(toInstall.Append(mod).ToArray(), opts, registry, game, crit))
                    {
                        // Child call will emit debug output, so we don't need to here
                        return true;
                    }
                }
                log.Debug($"Can't install {request}: Can't install provider of {k.requested}");
            }

Now I see a very important part! Look at lines 1600-1609:

```csharp
var checkedRecs = resolver.Recommendations(recommenders)
                          .Except(exclude)
                          .Where(m => resolver.ReasonsFor(m)
                                              .Any(r => r is SelectionReason.Recommended { ProvidesIndex: 0 }))

                                           registry, instance.Game, crit)
                      .ConflictList.Keys;
// Don't check recommendations that conflict with installed or installing mods
checkedRecs.ExceptWith(conflicting);
```

This code takes the recommendations from the resolver, then runs a second resolver to check which ones conflict, and removes those from `checkedRecs`. 

But wait - the first resolver (line 1588) uses `KitchenSinkOpts` which has `proceed_with_inconsistencies = true` AND `with_recommends = true`. So it should already include conflicting recommendations and record conflicts.

Then the second resolver (line 1604) uses `ConflictsOpts` which has `proceed_with_inconsistencies = true` but `with_recommends = false`. It checks which of the recommended mods conflict with the mods to install.

With my fix, the first resolver's `Recommendations` method should now include ALL recommended mods, even those that conflict with each other. Previously, conflicting recommended mods were silently excluded from `modlist`, so they wouldn't appear in `Recommendations()` either.

But there's another issue: the `Recommendations` method (lines 506-511):

```csharp
public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Recommendations(HashSet<CkanModule> dependencies)
    => modlist.Values.Except(dependencies)
                     .Where(m => ValidRecSugReasons(dependencies,
                                                    ReasonsFor(m).OfType<SelectionReason.Recommended>()
                                                                 .ToArray()))
                     .OrderByDescending(totalDependers);
```

This filters `modlist.Values` to only include mods that have a `Recommended` reason where the parent is in `dependencies`. Since my change adds conflicting recommended mods to `modlist` with the proper reason, they should now appear in `Recommendations()`.

But wait, there's a problem: the `ValidRecSugReasons` method at lines 522-526:

```csharp
private bool ValidRecSugReasons(HashSet<CkanModule>                  dependencies,
                                SelectionReason.RelationshipReason[] recSugReasons)
    => recSugReasons.Any(r => dependencies.Contains(r.Parent))
       && !suppressedRecommenders.Any(rel => recSugReasons.Any(r => r.Parent != null
                                                                       && rel.WithinBounds(r.Parent)));
```

This checks that at least one of the reasons has a parent in `dependencies`. Since we add the recommended mod with the proper `SelectionReason.Recommended` reason (with the correct parent), this should still work.

But there's another subtlety: in `ResolveStanza`, when we encounter a recommended mod that conflicts, we call `Add(candidate, reason)` where `reason` is the `SelectionReason.Recommended` or `SelectionReason.Suggested`. This should properly set up the reason so that `ValidRecSugReasons` can find it.

Let me trace through the logic to make sure:

1. User requests mod A
2. A has recommends: [B, C]
3. B and C conflict with each other
4. Processing A's recommends:
   - B is added to modlist with reason Recommended(A, 0)
   - C conflicts with B (already in modlist)
   - With my fix: C is added to modlist with reason Recommended(A, 1) (since it's the second recommended)
   - conflict is recorded

Now, `Recommendations({A})` will:
- Include B because it has reason Recommended(A, 0) and A is in dependencies
- Include C because it has reason Recommended(A, 1) and A is in dependencies

Both should appear. 

Now let me check the `Recommendations` method more carefully. It calls `ValidRecSugReasons` with the reasons. The reason for B is `Recommended(A, 0)` - parent is A, which is in dependencies. The reason for C is `Recommended(A, 1)` - parent is A, which is in dependencies. Both valid.

But wait, I need to check if there's an issue with the `Recommended` reason's index. Looking at line 171:

```csharp
ResolveStanza(module.recommends, new SelectionReason.Recommended(module, 0),
              options.get_recommenders ? options.WithoutRecommendations()
                                       : options.WithoutSuggestions(),
              true, old_stanza);
```

The reason is `Recommended(module, 0)` for ALL recommended mods of the same parent. But then there's special handling at lines 302-309:

```csharp
if (options.get_recommenders && reason is not SelectionReason.Depends)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < candidates.Count; ++i)
    {
        Add(candidates[i], reason is SelectionReason.Recommended rec
                               ? rec.WithIndex(i)
                               : reason);
    }
    continue;
}
```

This only applies when `get_recommenders` is true and there are multiple candidates. The index is used for `ProvidesIndex`.

But for the normal case (not `get_recommenders`), all recommended mods from the same parent get `Recommended(parent, 0)`. That should still work for `ValidRecSugReasons`.

    41	                    tabController.RenameTab(WaitTabPage.Name, Properties.Resources.MainImportWaitTitle);
    42	                    ShowWaitDialog();
    43	                    DisableMainWindow();
    44	                    Wait.StartWaiting(
    45	                        (sender, e) =>
    46	                        {
    47	                            if (e != null && Manager?.Cache != null && ManageMods.MainModList != null)
    48	                            {
    49	                                e.Result = ModuleImporter.ImportFiles(
    50	                                    GetFiles(dlg.FileNames),

    57	                                                                   out DataGridViewRow? row)

    61	                                        }
    62	                                    },
    63	                                    RegistryManager.Instance(CurrentInstance, repoData).registry,
    64	                                    CurrentInstance, Manager.Cache);
    65	                            }
    66	                        },
    67	                        (sender, e) =>
    68	                        {
    69	                            EnableMainWindow();
    70	                            if (e?.Error == null && e?.Result is bool result && result)
    71	                            {
    72	                                // Put GUI back the way we found it
    73	                                HideWaitDialog();
    74	                            }
    75	                            else
    76	                            {
    77	                                if (e?.Error is Exception exc)
    78	                                {
    79	                                    log.Error(exc.Message, exc);
    80	                                    currentUser.RaiseMessage("{0}", exc.Message);
    81	                                }
    82	                                Wait.Finish();
    83	                            }
    84	                        },
    85	                        false,
    86	                        null);
    87	                }
    88	            }

     1	using System;
     2	using System.IO;
     3	using System.Collections.Generic;
     4	using System.Linq;
     5	using System.Text.RegularExpressions;
     6	
     7	using ICSharpCode.SharpZipLib.Zip;
     8	using Newtonsoft.Json.Linq;
     9	using YamlDotNet.RepresentationModel;
    10	
    11	using CKAN.Extensions;
    12	using CKAN.Versioning;
    13	using CKAN.Avc;
    14	using CKAN.SpaceWarp;
    15	
    16	namespace CKAN.IO
    17	{
    18	    public static class ModuleImporter
    19	    {
    20	        /// <summary>
    21	        /// Import a list of files into the download cache, with progress bar and
    22	        /// interactive prompts for installation and deletion.
    23	        /// </summary>
    24	        /// <param name="files">Set of files to import</param>
    25	        /// <param name="user">Object for user interaction</param>
    26	        /// <param name="installMod">Function to call to mark a mod for installation</param>
    27	        /// <param name="registry">Registry to use for version checking</param>
    28	        /// <param name="instance">Game instance to use for version checking</param>
    29	        /// <param name="Cache">Cache to use for storing files</param>
    30	        /// <param name="allowDelete">True to ask user whether to delete imported files, false to leave the files as is</param>
    31	        public static bool ImportFiles(HashSet<FileInfo>  files,
    32	                                       IUser              user,
    33	                                       Action<CkanModule> installMod,
    34	                                       Registry           registry,
    35	                                       GameInstance       instance,
    36	                                       NetModuleCache     Cache,
    37	                                       bool               allowDelete = true)
    38	        {
    39	            if (!TryGetFileModules(files, registry, Cache,
    40	                                   out Dictionary<FileInfo, List<CkanModule>> matched,
    41	                                   out List<FileInfo> notFound,
    42	                                   new ProgressImmediate<int>(p =>
    43	                                       user.RaiseProgress(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportScanningFiles,
    44	                                                          p))))
    45	            {
    46	                // We're not going to do anything, so let the user know they failed
    47	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportNotFound,
    48	                                string.Join(", ", notFound.Select(fi => fi.Name)));
    49	                return false;
    50	            }
    51	
    52	            if (notFound.Count > 0)
    53	            {
    54	                // At least one was found, so just warn about the rest
    55	                user.RaiseMessage(" ");
    56	                user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportNotFound,
    57	                                  string.Join(", ", notFound.Select(fi => fi.Name)));
    58	            }
    59	            var installable = matched.Values.SelectMany(modules => modules)
    60	                                            .Where(m => m.IsCompatible(instance.VersionCriteria()))
    61	                                            .ToHashSet();
    62	
    63	            var deletable = matched.Keys.ToList();
    64	            var delete    = allowDelete
    65	                            && deletable.Count > 0
    66	                            && user.RaiseYesNoDialog(string.Format(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportDeletePrompt,
    67	                                                                   deletable.Count));
    68	
    69	            // Store once per "primary" URL since each has its own URL hash
    70	            var cachedGroups = matched.SelectMany(kvp => kvp.Value.DistinctBy(m => m.download?.First())
    71	                                                                  .Select(m => (File:   kvp.Key,
    72	                                                                                Module: m)))
    73	                                      .ToGroupedDictionary(tuple => Cache.IsMaybeCachedZip(tuple.Module));
    74	            if (cachedGroups.TryGetValue(true, out (FileInfo File, CkanModule Module)[]? alreadyStored))
    75	            {
    76	                // Notify about files that are already cached
    77	                user.RaiseMessage(" ");
    78	                user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportAlreadyCached,
    79	                                  string.Join(", ", alreadyStored.Select(tuple => $"{tuple.Module} ({tuple.File.Name})")));
    80	            }
    81	            if (cachedGroups.TryGetValue(false, out (FileInfo File, CkanModule Module)[]? toStore))
    82	            {
    83	                // Store any new files
    84	                user.RaiseMessage(" ");
    85	                var description = "";
    86	                long installedBytes = 0;
    87	                var rateCounter = new ByteRateCounter()
    88	                {
    89	                    Size      = toStore.Sum(tuple => tuple.File.Length),
    90	                    BytesLeft = toStore.Sum(tuple => tuple.File.Length),
    91	                };
    92	                rateCounter.Start();
    93	                var progress = new ProgressImmediate<long>(bytes =>
    94	                {
    95	                    rateCounter.BytesLeft = rateCounter.Size - (installedBytes + bytes);
    96	                    user.RaiseProgress(rateCounter);
    97	                });
    98	                foreach ((FileInfo fi, CkanModule module) in toStore)
    99	                {
   100	
   101	                    // Update the progress string
   102	                    description = $"{module} ({fi.Name})";
   103	                    Cache.Store(module, fi.FullName, progress,
   104	                                // Move if user said we could delete and we don't need to make any more copies
   105	                                move: delete && toStore.Last(tuple => tuple.File == fi).Module == module,
   106	                                // Skip revalidation because we had to check the hashes to get here!
   107	                                validate: false);
   108	                    installedBytes += fi.Length;
   109	                }
   110	                rateCounter.Stop();
   111	            }
   112	
   113	            // Here we have installable containing mods that can be installed, and the importable files have been stored in cache.
   114	            if (installable.Count > 0
   115	                && user.RaiseYesNoDialog(string.Format(Properties.Resources.ModuleInstallerImportInstallPrompt,
   116	                                                       installable.Count,
   117	                                                       instance.Name,
   118	                                                       instance.GameDir)))
   119	            {
   120	                // Install the imported mods
   121	                foreach (var mod in installable)
   122	                {
   123	                    installMod(mod);
   124	                }
   125	            }
   126	            if (delete)
   127	            {
   128	                // Delete old files that weren't already moved into cache
   129	                foreach (var f in deletable.Where(f => f.Exists))
   130	                {
   131	                    f.Delete();
   132	                }
   133	            }
   134	
   135	            return true;
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        private static bool TryGetFileModules(HashSet<FileInfo>                          files,
   139	                                              Registry                                   registry,
   140	                                              NetModuleCache                             Cache,
   141	                                              out Dictionary<FileInfo, List<CkanModule>> matched,
   142	                                              out List<FileInfo>                         notFound,
   143	                                              IProgress<int>                             percentProgress)
   144	        {
   145	            matched      = new Dictionary<FileInfo, List<CkanModule>>();
   146	            notFound     = new List<FileInfo>();
   147	            var index    = registry.GetDownloadHashesIndex();
   148	            var progress = new ProgressScalePercentsByFileSizes(percentProgress,
   149	                                                                files.Select(fi => fi.Length));
   150	            foreach (var fi in files.Distinct())
   151	            {
   152	                if (index.TryGetValue(Cache.GetFileHashSha256(fi.FullName, progress),
   153	                                      out List<CkanModule>? modules)
   154	                    // The progress bar will jump back and "redo" the same span
   155	                    // for non-matched files, but that's... OK?
   156	                    || index.TryGetValue(Cache.GetFileHashSha1(fi.FullName, progress),
   157	                                         out modules))
   158	                {
   159	                    matched.Add(fi, modules);
   160	                }
   161	                else if (GetInternalModules(new ZipFile(fi.FullName)).ToList() is var ckans
   162	                         && ckans.Count > 0)
   163	                {
   164	                    matched.Add(fi, ckans);
   165	                }
   166	                else
   167	                {
   168	                    notFound.Add(fi);
   169	                }
   170	                progress.NextFile();
   171	            }
   172	            return matched.Count > 0;
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        private static readonly Regex avcRegex    = new Regex(@"^#/ckan/ksp-avc(/(?<filter>.*))?$",
   176	                                                              RegexOptions.Compiled);
   177	
   178	        private static readonly Regex swInfoRegex = new Regex(@"^#/ckan/space-warp(/(?<filter>.*))?$",
   179	                                                              RegexOptions.Compiled);
   180	
   181	        private static IEnumerable<CkanModule> GetInternalModules(ZipFile zip)
   182	        {
   183	            var internalCkans = InternalCkanFiles(zip).ToArray();
   184	            // CkanModule.download is required for cache management, set a default if missing
   185	            foreach (var ckan in internalCkans)
   186	            {
   187	                ckan["download"] ??= $"https://ckan/imported-from-zip/{ckan["identifier"]}/{zip.Name}";
   188	            }
   189	            // Set the version and compatibility if we can
   190	            foreach (var grp in internalCkans.GroupBy(ckan => (string?)ckan["$vref"] ?? ""))
   191	            {
   192	                if (avcRegex.TryMatch(grp.Key, out Match? avcMatch))
   193	                {
   194	                    var filter = avcMatch.Groups["filter"].Success
   195	                                     ? avcMatch.Groups["filter"].ToString()
   196	                                     : null;
   197	                    ApplyAvcs(InternalVersionFiles(zip, filter).ToArray(), grp);
   198	                }
   199	                else if (swInfoRegex.TryMatch(grp.Key, out Match? swInfoMatch))
   200	                {
   201	                    var filter = swInfoMatch.Groups["filter"].Success
   202	                                     ? swInfoMatch.Groups["filter"].ToString()
   203	                                     : null;
   204	                    ApplySpaceWarpInfos(InternalSpaceWarpInfos(zip, filter).ToArray(), grp);
   205	                }
   206	            }
   207	            return internalCkans.Select(json => json.ToObject<CkanModule>())
   208	                                .OfType<CkanModule>();
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        private static void ApplyAvcs(AvcVersion[]         avcs,
   212	                                      IEnumerable<JObject> ckans)
   213	        {
   214	            if (avcs.Length > 1)
   215	            {
   216	                throw new Kraken(string.Format("Too many .version files found!"));
   217	            }
   218	            foreach (var avc in avcs)
   219	            {
   220	                foreach (var ckan in ckans)
   221	                {
   222	                    ckan.Remove("$vref");
   223	                    if (avc.version is ModuleVersion ver)
   224	                    {
   225	                        ckan["version"] ??= ver.ToString();
   226	                    }
   227	                    GameVersion.SetJsonCompatibility(ckan, avc.ksp_version,
   228	                                                           avc.ksp_version_min,
   229	                                                           avc.ksp_version_max);
   230	                }
   231	            }
   232	        }
   233	
   234	        private static void ApplySpaceWarpInfos(SpaceWarpInfo[]      swInfos,
   235	                                                IEnumerable<JObject> ckans)
   236	        {
   237	            if (swInfos.Length > 1)
   238	            {
   239	                throw new Kraken(string.Format("Too many swinfo.json files found!"));
   240	            }
   241	            foreach (var swInfo in swInfos)
   242	            {
   243	                bool hasMin = GameVersion.TryParse(swInfo.ksp2_version?.min, out GameVersion? minVer);
   244	                bool hasMax = GameVersion.TryParse(swInfo.ksp2_version?.max, out GameVersion? maxVer);
   245	                foreach (var ckan in ckans)
   246	                {
   247	                    ckan.Remove("$vref");
   248	                    ckan["version"] ??= swInfo.version;
   249	                    if (hasMin || hasMax)
   250	                    {
   251	                        GameVersion.SetJsonCompatibility(ckan, null,
   252	                                                               minVer?.WithoutBuild,
   253	                                                               maxVer?.WithoutBuild);
   254	                    }
   255	                }
   256	            }
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        private static IEnumerable<JObject> InternalCkanFiles(ZipFile zip)
   260	            => GetInternalYamlFiles(zip, ".ckan", null);
   261	
   262	        private static IEnumerable<AvcVersion> InternalVersionFiles(ZipFile zip, string? filter)
   263	            => GetInternalJsonFiles(zip, ".version", filter)
   264	                   .Select(json => json.ToObject<AvcVersion>())
   265	                   .OfType<AvcVersion>();
   266	
   267	        private static IEnumerable<SpaceWarpInfo> InternalSpaceWarpInfos(ZipFile zip, string? filter)
   268	            => GetInternalJsonFiles(zip, "swinfo.json", filter)
   269	                   .Select(json => json.ToObject<SpaceWarpInfo>())
   270	                   .OfType<SpaceWarpInfo>();
   271	
   272	        private static IEnumerable<JObject> GetInternalYamlFiles(ZipFile zip, string nameSuffix, string? filter)
   273	            => FilterEntries(zip, nameSuffix, filter)
   274	                   .SelectMany(entry =>
   275	                               {
   276	                                   var stream = new YamlStream();
   277	                                   stream.Load(new StreamReader(zip.GetInputStream(entry)));
   278	                                   return stream.Documents.Select(doc => doc?.RootNode)
   279	                                                          .OfType<YamlMappingNode>()
   280	                                                          .Select(yaml => yaml.ToJObject());
   281	                               });
   282	
   283	        private static IEnumerable<JObject> GetInternalJsonFiles(ZipFile zip, string nameSuffix, string? filter)
   284	            => FilterEntries(zip, nameSuffix, filter)
   285	                   .Select(entry => JObject.Parse(new StreamReader(zip.GetInputStream(entry)).ReadToEnd()));
   286	
   287	        private static IEnumerable<ZipEntry> FilterEntries(ZipFile zip, string nameSuffix, string? filter)
   288	            => zip.OfType<ZipEntry>()
   289	                  .Where(entry => entry.Name.EndsWith(nameSuffix, StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase)
   290	                                  && (filter == null
   291	                                      || entry.Name == filter
   292	                                      || Regex.IsMatch(entry.Name, filter)));

     1	using System;
     2	using System.IO;
     3	using System.Collections.Generic;
     4	using System.Linq;
     5	
     6	using CommandLine;
     7	using log4net;
     8	
     9	using CKAN.IO;
    10	
    11	namespace CKAN.CmdLine
    12	{
    13	    public class Install : ICommand
    14	    {
    15	        /// <summary>
    16	        /// Initialize the install command object
    17	        /// </summary>
    18	        /// <param name="mgr">GameInstanceManager containing our instances</param>
    19	        /// <param name="user">IUser object for interaction</param>
    20	        public Install(GameInstanceManager mgr, RepositoryDataManager repoData, IUser user)
    21	        {
    22	            manager       = mgr;
    23	            this.repoData = repoData;
    24	            this.user     = user;
    25	        }
    26	
    27	        /// <summary>
    28	        /// Installs a module, if available
    29	        /// </summary>
    30	        /// <param name="instance">Game instance into which to install</param>
    31	        /// <param name="raw_options">Command line options object</param>
    32	        /// <returns>
    33	        /// Exit code for shell environment
    34	        /// </returns>
    35	        public int RunCommand(CKAN.GameInstance instance, object raw_options)
    36	        {
    37	            RegistryManager.Instance(instance, repoData).ScanUnmanagedFiles();
    38	
    39	            var options = raw_options as InstallOptions;
    40	            if (options?.modules?.Count == 0 && options.ckan_files == null)
    41	            {
    42	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
    43	                foreach (var h in Actions.GetHelp("install"))
    44	                {
    45	                    user.RaiseError("{0}", h);
    46	                }
    47	                return Exit.BADOPT;
    48	            }
    49	
    50	            var regMgr = RegistryManager.Instance(instance, repoData);
    51	            List<CkanModule>? modules = null;
    52	
    53	            if (options?.ckan_files != null)
    54	            {
    55	                // Install from CKAN files
    56	                try
    57	                {
    58	                    var targets = options.ckan_files
    59	                                         .Select(arg => new NetAsyncDownloader.DownloadTargetFile(getUri(arg)))
    60	                                         .ToArray();
    61	                    log.DebugFormat("Urls: {0}", targets.SelectMany(t => t.urls));
    62	                    new NetAsyncDownloader(new NullUser(), () => null, options.NetUserAgent).DownloadAndWait(targets);
    63	                    log.DebugFormat("Files: {0}", targets.Select(t => t.filename));
    64	                    modules = targets.Select(t => CkanModule.FromFile(t.filename))
    65	                                     .ToList();
    66	                }
    67	                catch (FileNotFoundKraken kraken)
    68	                {
    69	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstallNotFound,
    70	                                    kraken.file ?? "");
    71	                    return Exit.ERROR;
    72	                }
    73	                catch (Kraken kraken)
    74	                {
    75	                    user.RaiseError("{0}",
    76	                        kraken.InnerException == null
    77	                            ? kraken.Message
    78	                            : $"{kraken.Message}: {kraken.InnerException.Message}");
    79	                    return Exit.ERROR;
    80	                }
    81	            }
    82	            else
    83	            {
    84	                var identifiers = options?.modules ?? new List<string> { };
    85	                var registry    = regMgr.registry;
    86	                var installed   = registry.InstalledModules
    87	                                          .Select(im => im.Module)
    88	                                          .ToArray();
    89	                var crit        = instance.VersionCriteria();
    90	                Search.AdjustModulesCase(instance, registry, identifiers);
    91	                modules = identifiers.Select(arg => CkanModule.FromIDandVersion(
    92	                                                        registry, arg,
    93	                                                        (options?.allow_incompatible ?? false)
    94	                                                            ? null
    95	                                                            : crit)
    96	                                                    ?? registry.LatestAvailable(arg,
    97	                                                                                instance.StabilityToleranceConfig,
    98	                                                                                crit, null, installed)
    99	                                                    ?? registry.InstalledModule(arg)?.Module)
   100	                                     .OfType<CkanModule>()
   101	                                     .ToList();
   102	            }
   103	
   104	            if (manager.Cache == null)
   105	            {
   106	                return Exit.ERROR;
   107	            }
   108	
   109	            var installer   = new ModuleInstaller(instance, manager.Cache,
   110	                                                  manager.Configuration, user);
   111	            var install_ops = new RelationshipResolverOptions(instance.StabilityToleranceConfig)
   112	            {
   113	                with_all_suggests              = options?.with_all_suggests ?? false,
   114	                with_suggests                  = options?.with_suggests ?? false,
   115	                with_recommends                = !options?.no_recommends ?? true,
   116	                allow_incompatible             = options?.allow_incompatible ?? false,
   117	                without_toomanyprovides_kraken = user.Headless,
   118	                without_enforce_consistency    = user.Headless,
   119	            };
   120	
   121	            var autoInstalled = new HashSet<CkanModule>();
   122	            for (bool done = false; !done; )
   123	            {
   124	                // Install everything requested. :)
   125	                try
   126	                {
   127	                    HashSet<string>? possibleConfigOnlyDirs = null;
   128	                    installer.InstallList(modules, install_ops, regMgr,
   129	                                          ref possibleConfigOnlyDirs,
   130	                                          new InstalledFilesDeduplicator(instance,
   131	                                                                         manager.Instances.Values,
   132	                                                                         repoData),
   133	                                          options?.NetUserAgent,
   134	                                          null, autoInstalled);
   135	                    user.RaiseMessage("");
   136	                    done = true;
   137	                }
   138	                catch (TooManyModsProvideKraken ex)
   139	                {
   140	                    // Request the user selects one of the mods
   141	                    int result;
   142	                    var choices = ex.modules.OrderByDescending(m => repoData.GetDownloadCount(regMgr.registry.Repositories.Values,
   143	                                                                                              m.identifier)
   144	                                                                    ?? 0)
   145	                                            .ThenByDescending(m => m.identifier == ex.requested)
   146	                                            .ThenBy(m => m.identifier)
   147	                                            .ToArray();
   148	                    try
   149	                    {
   150	                        result = user.RaiseSelectionDialog(
   151	                            ex.Message,
   152	                            choices.Select(m => string.Format("{0} ({1})",
   153	                                                              m.identifier, m.name))
   154	                                   .ToArray());
   155	                    }
   156	                    catch (Kraken e)
   157	                    {
   158	                        user.RaiseMessage("{0}", e.Message);
   159	                        return Exit.ERROR;
   160	                    }
   161	
   162	                    if (result < 0)
   163	                    {
   164	                        user.RaiseMessage("");
   165	                        return Exit.ERROR;
   166	                    }
   167	
   168	                    // Add the module to the list.
   169	                    modules.Add(choices[result]);
   170	                    autoInstalled.Add(choices[result]);
   171	                    // DON'T return so we can loop around and try again
   172	                }
   173	                catch (CancelledActionKraken k)
   174	                {
   175	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstallAborted,
   176	                                    k.Message);
   177	                    return Exit.ERROR;
   178	                }
   179	                catch (RequestThrottledKraken kraken)
   180	                {
   181	                    user.RaiseError("{0}", kraken.Message);
   182	                    user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstallTryAuthToken,
   183	                                      kraken.infoUrl);
   184	                    return Exit.ERROR;
   185	                }
   186	                catch (Kraken kraken)
   187	                {
   188	                    // Show nice message for mod problems
   189	                    user.RaiseError("{0}", kraken.Message);
   190	                    user.RaiseMessage("{0}", kraken switch
   191	                    {
   192	                        DependenciesNotSatisfiedKraken or ModuleNotFoundKraken => Properties.Resources.InstallTryAgain,
   193	                        _ => Properties.Resources.InstallCancelled,
   194	                    });
   195	                    return Exit.ERROR;
   196	                }
   197	                catch (Exception exc)
   198	                {
   199	                    // Show stack trace for code problems
   200	                    user.RaiseError("{0}", exc.ToString());
   201	                    user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstallCancelled);
   202	                    return Exit.ERROR;
   203	                }
   204	            }
   205	
   206	            return Exit.OK;
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        private static Uri getUri(string arg)
   210	            => Uri.IsWellFormedUriString(arg, UriKind.Absolute)
   211	                ? new Uri(arg)
   212	                : File.Exists(arg)
   213	                    ? new Uri(Path.GetFullPath(arg))
   214	                    : throw new FileNotFoundKraken(arg);
   215	
   216	        private readonly GameInstanceManager   manager;
   217	        private readonly RepositoryDataManager repoData;
   218	        private readonly IUser                 user;
   219	
   220	        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(Install));
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    internal class InstallOptions : InstanceSpecificOptions
   224	    {
   225	        [OptionArray('c', "ckanfiles", HelpText = "Local CKAN files or URLs to process")]
   226	        public string[]? ckan_files { get; set; }
   227	
   228	        [Option("no-recommends", DefaultValue = false, HelpText = "Do not install recommended modules")]
   229	        public bool no_recommends { get; set; }
   230	
   231	        [Option("with-suggests", DefaultValue = false, HelpText = "Install suggested modules")]
   232	        public bool with_suggests { get; set; }
   233	
   234	        [Option("with-all-suggests", DefaultValue = false, HelpText = "Install suggested modules all the way down")]
   235	        public bool with_all_suggests { get; set; }
   236	
   237	        [Option("allow-incompatible", DefaultValue = false, HelpText = "Install modules that are not compatible with the current game version")]
   238	        public bool allow_incompatible { get; set; }
   239	
   240	        [ValueList(typeof(List<string>))]
   241	        [AvailableIdentifiers]
   242	        public List<string>? modules { get; set; }
   243	    }
   244	
   245	}

At line 111-119, the install command creates `RelationshipResolverOptions` with `with_recommends = !options?.no_recommends ?? true` (so recommends are enabled by default) and `proceed_with_inconsistencies` is NOT set (defaults to false). \n\nSo when installing from a ckan file with recommends:\n- `with_recommends = true`\n- `proceed_with_inconsistencies = false`\n- `soft_resolve = true` for recommends\n\nWith the old code: conflicting recommended mods are silently excluded → BUG\nWith my fix: conflicting recommended mods are added and conflicts recorded → FIX\n\nThis matches the PR description exactly!\n\nNow let me verify there aren't any other issues. Let me also check if there's a similar problem in the first pass of `AddModulesToInstall` for user-requested modules. Looking at lines 94-114:\n\n```csharp\n// This part can't be parallel, to preserve order of processing\nforeach (CkanModule module in modules)\n{\n    // Need to check against installed mods and those to install.\n    var conflictingModules = modlist.Values\n                                    .Concat(installed_modules)\n                                    .Where(listed_mod => listed_mod.ConflictsWith(module));\n    foreach (CkanModule listed_mod in conflictingModules)\n    {\n        if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)\n        {\n            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(listed_mod, module));\n            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(module, listed_mod));\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            throw new InconsistentKraken(...);\n        }\n    }\n\n    user_requested_mods.Add(module);\n    Add(module, new SelectionReason.UserRequested());\n}\n```\n\nFor user-requested modules, if there's a conflict between two of them, it either records the conflict or throws. It doesn't silently exclude one. So that's fine.\n\nBut what about the PR's scenario where the user has a ckan file with recommends that conflict? The user-requested modules are from the ckan file (the main module being installed). That module gets added first. Then its recommends are processed via `ResolveStanza` with `soft_resolve = true`. If two recommended mods conflict, the first one gets added, and the second one would (with my fix) also get added with a conflict recorded.\n\nLet me also double-check that the `Recommendations` method will properly return ALL recommended mods, including conflicting ones. The method is:\n\n```csharp\npublic IEnumerable<CkanModule> Recommendations(HashSet<CkanModule> dependencies)\n    => modlist.Values.Except(dependencies)\n                     .Where(m => ValidRecSugReasons(dependencies,\n                                                    ReasonsFor(m).OfType<SelectionReason.Recommended>()\n                                                                 .ToArray()))\n                     .OrderByDescending(totalDependers);\n```\n\nThis should work because:\n1. Conflicting recommended mods are now in `modlist.Values`\n2. They have `SelectionReason.Recommended` reasons with the correct parent\n3. They are not in `dependencies` (which are the hard dependencies)\n4. `ValidRecSugReasons` checks that at least one reason's parent is in `dependencies`\n\nSo `Recommendations` should return them.\n\nNow I'm confident my change is correct. Let me also think about potential side effects:\n\n1. **SanityChecker**: At lines 127-137, `SanityChecker.EnforceConsistency` is called. This might throw `BadRelationshipsKraken` because of the conflicting mods now in `modlist`. But if `without_enforce_consistency` is set, it catches the exception and adds the conflicts. If `without_enforce_consistency` is not set, it would throw. But for recommends/suggests, the calling code typically sets `without_enforce_consistency = true` when it wants to handle conflicts gracefully.\n\n2. **The `Resolve` method**: When a recommended mod conflicts, we add it but don't call `Resolve` on it. This means its own dependencies/recommendations won't be processed. This is consistent with the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` behavior. If we wanted to also resolve its dependencies, we'd need to add a `Resolve` call. But for now, I'll keep it minimal.\n\nActually, wait. Let me reconsider whether we should call `Resolve` in the soft_resolve conflict case. The reason is:\n\nIf a recommended mod has hard dependencies, those should still be pulled in even if the recommended mod conflicts with something. Otherwise, the user might try to select that recommended mod later and find it can't be installed because of missing dependencies.\n\nBut looking at the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` case (line 356-361), it also doesn't call `Resolve`. So maybe this is intentional - if there's a conflict, the solution is already broken, so there's no point in resolving further.\n\nFor the PR's issue, the fix doesn't need to resolve dependencies of conflicting recommended mods. The PR just asks for all recommended mods to be listed.\n\nI'm going to keep my fix minimal. Let me also check if the `Suggestions` method has similar issues - it uses `ValidRecSugReasons` too and should now include conflicting suggested mods as well.\n\nLet me make sure the fix is complete and then submit.\n\nActually, let me also check one more thing: the `Dependencies` method:\n\n```csharp\npublic IEnumerable<CkanModule> Dependencies()\n    => BreadthFirstSearch(user_requested_mods.Where(m => !suppressedRecommenders.Any(rel => rel.WithinBounds(m))),\n                          (searching, found) =>\n                              modlist.Values\n                                     .Except(found)\n                                     .Where(m => ReasonsFor(m).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.Depends dep\n                                                                        && dep.Parent == searching)));\n```\n\nThis only returns hard dependencies (those with `SelectionReason.Depends` reasons).
```csharp
// This part can't be parallel, to preserve order of processing
foreach (CkanModule module in modules)
{
    // Need to check against installed mods and those to install.
    var conflictingModules = modlist.Values
                                    .Concat(installed_modules)
                                    .Where(listed_mod => listed_mod.ConflictsWith(module));
    foreach (CkanModule listed_mod in conflictingModules)
    {
        if (options.proceed_with_inconsistencies)
        {
            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(listed_mod, module));
            conflicts.Add(new ModPair(module, listed_mod));
        }
        else
        {
            throw new InconsistentKraken(...);
        }
    }

    user_requested_mods.Add(module);
    Add(module, new SelectionReason.UserRequested());
}
```

For user-requested modules, if there's a conflict between two of them, it either records the conflict or throws. It doesn't silently exclude one. So that's fine.

But what about the PR's scenario where the user has a ckan file with recommends that conflict? The user-requested modules are from the ckan file (the main module being installed). That module gets added first. Then its recommends are processed via `ResolveStanza` with `soft_resolve = true`. If two recommended mods conflict, the first one gets added, and the second one would (with my fix) also get added with a conflict recorded.

Let me also double-check that the `Recommendations` method will properly return ALL recommended mods, including conflicting ones. The method is:

```csharp
public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Recommendations(HashSet<CkanModule> dependencies)
    => modlist.Values.Except(dependencies)
                     .Where(m => ValidRecSugReasons(dependencies,
                                                    ReasonsFor(m).OfType<SelectionReason.Recommended>()
                                                                 .ToArray()))
                     .OrderByDescending(totalDependers);
```

This should work because:
1. Conflicting recommended mods are now in `modlist.Values`
2. They have `SelectionReason.Recommended` reasons with the correct parent
3. They are not in `dependencies` (which are the hard dependencies)
4. `ValidRecSugReasons` checks that at least one reason's parent is in `dependencies`

So `Recommendations` should return them.

1. **SanityChecker**: At lines 127-137, `SanityChecker.EnforceConsistency` is called. This might throw `BadRelationshipsKraken` because of the conflicting mods now in `modlist`. But if `without_enforce_consistency` is set, it catches the exception and adds the conflicts. If `without_enforce_consistency` is not set, it would throw. But for recommends/suggests, the calling code typically sets `without_enforce_consistency = true` when it wants to handle conflicts gracefully.

2. **The `Resolve` method**: When a recommended mod conflicts, we add it but don't call `Resolve` on it. This means its own dependencies/recommendations won't be processed. This is consistent with the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` behavior. If we wanted to also resolve its dependencies, we'd need to add a `Resolve` call. But for now, I'll keep it minimal.

Actually, wait. Let me reconsider whether we should call `Resolve` in the soft_resolve conflict case. The reason is:

If a recommended mod has hard dependencies, those should still be pulled in even if the recommended mod conflicts with something. Otherwise, the user might try to select that recommended mod later and find it can't be installed because of missing dependencies.

But looking at the `proceed_with_inconsistencies` case (line 356-361), it also doesn't call `Resolve`. So maybe this is intentional - if there's a conflict, the solution is already broken, so there's no point in resolving further.

For the PR's issue, the fix doesn't need to resolve dependencies of conflicting recommended mods. The PR just asks for all recommended mods to be listed.

```csharp
public IEnumerable<CkanModule> Dependencies()
    => BreadthFirstSearch(user_requested_mods.Where(m => !suppressedRecommenders.Any(rel => rel.WithinBounds(m))),
                          (searching, found) =>
                              modlist.Values
                                     .Except(found)
                                     .Where(m => ReasonsFor(m).Any(r => r is SelectionReason.Depends dep
                                                                        && dep.Parent == searching)));
```

2026-05-29 15:21:10,213 - ERROR - swea-env-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4561 - Command failed:
